                - paragraph [ref=e208]:
                  - text: Canceling a running Workflow Execution records a
                  - code [ref=e209]: WorkflowExecutionCancelRequested
                  - text: event in the Event History. The Service schedules a new Command Task, and the Workflow Execution performs any cleanup work supported by its implementation.
                - paragraph [ref=e210]: "Use the Workflow ID to cancel an Execution:"
                - generic [ref=e212]:
                  - code [ref=e214]:
                    - generic [ref=e215]: temporal workflow cancel \
                    - generic [ref=e216]: "--workflow-id YourWorkflowId"
                  - button "Copy code to clipboard" [ref=e218] [cursor=pointer]:
                    - generic [ref=e219]:
                      - img [ref=e220]

                - generic [ref=e226]:
                  - code [ref=e228]:
                    - generic [ref=e229]: temporal workflow cancel \
                    - generic [ref=e230]: "--query YourQuery"
                  - button "Copy code to clipboard" [ref=e232] [cursor=pointer]:

                  - text: to read more about Search Attributes and Query creation. See
                  - code [ref=e240]: temporal batch --help
                  - text: for a quick reference.
                - paragraph [ref=e241]: Use the following options to change the behavior of this command.
                - paragraph [ref=e242]:
                  - strong [ref=e243]: "Flags:"
                - paragraph [ref=e244]:
                  - strong [ref=e245]: "--query"
                  - text: ","
                  - strong [ref=e246]: "-q"
                  - emphasis [ref=e247]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e248]:
                  - text: Content for an SQL-like
                  - code [ref=e249]: QUERY
                  - text: List Filter. You must set either --workflow-id or --query.
                - paragraph [ref=e250]:
                  - strong [ref=e251]: "--reason"
                  - emphasis [ref=e252]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e253]: Reason for batch operation. Only use with --query. Defaults to user name.
                - paragraph [ref=e254]:
                  - strong [ref=e255]: "--rps"
                  - emphasis [ref=e256]: float
                - paragraph [ref=e257]: Limit batch's requests per second. Only allowed if query is present.
                - paragraph [ref=e258]:
                  - strong [ref=e259]: "--run-id"
                  - text: ","
                  - strong [ref=e260]: "-r"
                  - emphasis [ref=e261]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e262]: Run ID. Only use with --workflow-id. Cannot use with --query.
                - paragraph [ref=e263]:
                  - strong [ref=e264]: "--workflow-id"
                  - text: ","
                  - strong [ref=e265]: "-w"
                  - emphasis [ref=e266]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e267]: Workflow ID. You must set either --workflow-id or --query.
                - paragraph [ref=e268]:
                  - strong [ref=e269]: "--yes"
                  - text: ","
                  - strong [ref=e270]: "-y"
                  - emphasis [ref=e271]: bool
                - paragraph [ref=e272]: Don't prompt to confirm signaling. Only allowed when --query is present.
                - paragraph [ref=e273]:
                  - strong [ref=e274]: "Global Flags:"
                - paragraph [ref=e275]:
                  - strong [ref=e276]: "--address"
                  - emphasis [ref=e277]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e278]: Temporal Service gRPC endpoint. (default "localhost:7233")
                - paragraph [ref=e279]:
                  - strong [ref=e280]: "--api-key"
                  - emphasis [ref=e281]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e282]: API key for request.
                - paragraph [ref=e283]:
                  - strong [ref=e284]: "--client-authority"
                  - emphasis [ref=e285]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e286]: Temporal gRPC client :authority pseudoheader.
                - paragraph [ref=e287]:
                  - strong [ref=e288]: "--client-connect-timeout"
                  - emphasis [ref=e289]: duration
                - paragraph [ref=e290]: The client connection timeout. 0s means no timeout.
                - paragraph [ref=e291]:
                  - strong [ref=e292]: "--codec-auth"
                  - emphasis [ref=e293]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e294]: Authorization header for Codec Server requests.
                - paragraph [ref=e295]:
                  - strong [ref=e296]: "--codec-endpoint"
                  - emphasis [ref=e297]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e298]: Remote Codec Server endpoint.
                - paragraph [ref=e299]:
                  - strong [ref=e300]: "--codec-header"
                  - emphasis [ref=e301]: string[]
                - paragraph [ref=e302]:
                  - text: HTTP headers for requests to codec server. Format as a
                  - code [ref=e303]: KEY=VALUE
                  - text: pair. May be passed multiple times to set multiple headers.
                - paragraph [ref=e304]:
                  - strong [ref=e305]: "--color"
                  - emphasis [ref=e306]: string-enum
                - paragraph [ref=e307]: "Output coloring. Accepted values: always, never, auto. (default \"auto\")"
                - paragraph [ref=e308]:
                  - strong [ref=e309]: "--command-timeout"
                  - emphasis [ref=e310]: duration
                - paragraph [ref=e311]: The command execution timeout. 0s means no timeout.
                - paragraph [ref=e312]:
                  - strong [ref=e313]: "--config-file"
                  - emphasis [ref=e314]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e315]:
                  - text: File path to read TOML config from, defaults to
                  - code [ref=e316]: $CONFIG_PATH/temporal/temporal.toml
                  - text: where
                  - code [ref=e317]: $CONFIG_PATH
                  - text: is defined as
                  - code [ref=e318]: $HOME/.config
                  - text: on Unix, "$HOME/Library/Application Support" on macOS, and %AppData% on Windows.
                - generic [ref=e319]:
                  - generic [ref=e320]:
                    - img [ref=e322]
                    - text: note
                  - paragraph [ref=e325]: Option is experimental.
                - paragraph [ref=e326]:
                  - strong [ref=e327]: "--disable-config-env"
                  - emphasis [ref=e328]: bool
                - paragraph [ref=e329]: If set, disables loading environment config from environment variables.
                - generic [ref=e330]:
                  - generic [ref=e331]:
                    - img [ref=e333]
                    - text: note
                  - paragraph [ref=e336]: Option is experimental.
                - paragraph [ref=e337]:
                  - strong [ref=e338]: "--disable-config-file"
                  - emphasis [ref=e339]: bool
                - paragraph [ref=e340]: If set, disables loading environment config from config file.
                - generic [ref=e341]:
                  - generic [ref=e342]:
                    - img [ref=e344]
                    - text: note
                  - paragraph [ref=e347]: Option is experimental.

                  - strong [ref=e349]: "--env"
                  - emphasis [ref=e350]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e351]:
                  - text: Active environment name (
                  - code [ref=e352]: ENV
                  - text: ). (default "default")
                - paragraph [ref=e353]:
                  - strong [ref=e354]: "--env-file"
                  - emphasis [ref=e355]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e356]:
                  - text: Path to environment settings file. Defaults to
                  - code [ref=e357]: $HOME/.config/temporalio/temporal.yaml
                  - text: .
                - paragraph [ref=e358]:
                  - strong [ref=e359]: "--grpc-meta"
                  - emphasis [ref=e360]: string[]
                - paragraph [ref=e361]:
                  - text: HTTP headers for requests. Format as a
                  - code [ref=e362]: KEY=VALUE
                  - text: pair. May be passed multiple times to set multiple headers. Can also be made available via environment variable as
                  - code [ref=e363]: TEMPORAL_GRPC_META_[name]

                - paragraph [ref=e364]:
                  - strong [ref=e365]: "--identity"
                  - emphasis [ref=e366]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e367]:
                  - text: "The identity of the user or client submitting this request. Defaults to \"temporal-cli:"
                  - generic [ref=e368]:
                    - math [ref=e370]:
                      - generic [ref=e372]:
                        - generic [ref=e373]: U
                        - generic [ref=e374]: S

                - paragraph [ref=e380]:
                  - strong [ref=e381]: "--log-format"

                - paragraph [ref=e383]: "Log format. Accepted values: text, json. (default \"text\")"
                - paragraph [ref=e384]:
                  - strong [ref=e385]: "--log-level"
                  - emphasis [ref=e386]: string-enum
                - paragraph [ref=e387]:
                  - text: Log level. Default is "info" for most commands and "warn" for
                  - code [ref=e388]: server start-dev
                  - text: ". Accepted values: debug, info, warn, error, never. (default \"info\")"
                - paragraph [ref=e389]:

                - paragraph [ref=e393]: Temporal Service Namespace. (default "default")
                - paragraph [ref=e394]:
                  - strong [ref=e395]: "--no-json-shorthand-payloads"
                  - emphasis [ref=e396]: bool
                - paragraph [ref=e397]: Raw payload output, even if the JSON option was used.

                  - strong [ref=e399]: "--output"
                  - text: ","
                  - strong [ref=e400]: "-o"
                  - emphasis [ref=e401]: string-enum
                - paragraph [ref=e402]: "Non-logging data output format. Accepted values: text, json, jsonl, none. (default \"text\")"
                - paragraph [ref=e403]:
                  - strong [ref=e404]: "--profile"
                  - emphasis [ref=e405]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e406]: Profile to use for config file.
                - generic [ref=e407]:
                  - generic [ref=e408]:
                    - img [ref=e410]
                    - text: note
                  - paragraph [ref=e413]: Option is experimental.
                - paragraph [ref=e414]:
                  - strong [ref=e415]: "--time-format"
                  - emphasis [ref=e416]: string-enum
                - paragraph [ref=e417]: "Time format. Accepted values: relative, iso, raw. (default \"relative\")"
                - paragraph [ref=e418]:
                  - strong [ref=e419]: "--tls"
                  - emphasis [ref=e420]: bool
                - paragraph [ref=e421]: Enable base TLS encryption. Does not have additional options like mTLS or client certs. This is defaulted to true if api-key or any other TLS options are present. Use --tls=false to explicitly disable.
                - paragraph [ref=e422]:
                  - strong [ref=e423]: "--tls-ca-data"
                  - emphasis [ref=e424]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e425]: Data for server CA certificate. Can't be used with --tls-ca-path.
                - paragraph [ref=e426]:
                  - strong [ref=e427]: "--tls-ca-path"
                  - emphasis [ref=e428]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e429]: Path to server CA certificate. Can't be used with --tls-ca-data.
                - paragraph [ref=e430]:
                  - strong [ref=e431]: "--tls-cert-data"
                  - emphasis [ref=e432]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e433]: Data for x509 certificate. Can't be used with --tls-cert-path.
                - paragraph [ref=e434]:
                  - strong [ref=e435]: "--tls-cert-path"
                  - emphasis [ref=e436]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e437]: Path to x509 certificate. Can't be used with --tls-cert-data.
                - paragraph [ref=e438]:
                  - strong [ref=e439]: "--tls-disable-host-verification"
                  - emphasis [ref=e440]: bool
                - paragraph [ref=e441]: Disable TLS host-name verification.
                - paragraph [ref=e442]:
                  - strong [ref=e443]: "--tls-key-data"
                  - emphasis [ref=e444]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e445]: Private certificate key data. Can't be used with --tls-key-path.
                - paragraph [ref=e446]:
                  - strong [ref=e447]: "--tls-key-path"
                  - emphasis [ref=e448]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e449]: Path to x509 private key. Can't be used with --tls-key-data.
                - paragraph [ref=e450]:
                  - strong [ref=e451]: "--tls-server-name"
                  - emphasis [ref=e452]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e453]: Override target TLS server name.

                  - emphasis [ref=e491]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e492]: API key for request.
                - paragraph [ref=e493]:
                  - strong [ref=e494]: "--client-authority"
                  - emphasis [ref=e495]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e496]: Temporal gRPC client :authority pseudoheader.
                - paragraph [ref=e497]:
                  - strong [ref=e498]: "--client-connect-timeout"
                  - emphasis [ref=e499]: duration
                - paragraph [ref=e500]: The client connection timeout. 0s means no timeout.
                - paragraph [ref=e501]:
                  - strong [ref=e502]: "--codec-auth"
                  - emphasis [ref=e503]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e504]: Authorization header for Codec Server requests.
                - paragraph [ref=e505]:
                  - strong [ref=e506]: "--codec-endpoint"
                  - emphasis [ref=e507]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e508]: Remote Codec Server endpoint.
                - paragraph [ref=e509]:
                  - strong [ref=e510]: "--codec-header"
                  - emphasis [ref=e511]: string[]
                - paragraph [ref=e512]:
                  - text: HTTP headers for requests to codec server. Format as a
                  - code [ref=e513]: KEY=VALUE
                  - text: pair. May be passed multiple times to set multiple headers.
                - paragraph [ref=e514]:
                  - strong [ref=e515]: "--color"
                  - emphasis [ref=e516]: string-enum
                - paragraph [ref=e517]: "Output coloring. Accepted values: always, never, auto. (default \"auto\")"
                - paragraph [ref=e518]:
                  - strong [ref=e519]: "--command-timeout"
                  - emphasis [ref=e520]: duration
                - paragraph [ref=e521]: The command execution timeout. 0s means no timeout.
                - paragraph [ref=e522]:
                  - strong [ref=e523]: "--config-file"
                  - emphasis [ref=e524]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e525]:
                  - text: File path to read TOML config from, defaults to
                  - code [ref=e526]: $CONFIG_PATH/temporal/temporal.toml
                  - text: where
                  - code [ref=e527]: $CONFIG_PATH
                  - text: is defined as
                  - code [ref=e528]: $HOME/.config
                  - text: on Unix, "$HOME/Library/Application Support" on macOS, and %AppData% on Windows.
                - generic [ref=e529]:
                  - generic [ref=e530]:
                    - img [ref=e532]
                    - text: note
                  - paragraph [ref=e535]: Option is experimental.
                - paragraph [ref=e536]:
                  - strong [ref=e537]: "--disable-config-env"
                  - emphasis [ref=e538]: bool
                - paragraph [ref=e539]: If set, disables loading environment config from environment variables.
                - generic [ref=e540]:
                  - generic [ref=e541]:
                    - img [ref=e543]
                    - text: note
                  - paragraph [ref=e546]: Option is experimental.
                - paragraph [ref=e547]:
                  - strong [ref=e548]: "--disable-config-file"
                  - emphasis [ref=e549]: bool
                - paragraph [ref=e550]: If set, disables loading environment config from config file.
                - generic [ref=e551]:
                  - generic [ref=e552]:
                    - img [ref=e554]
                    - text: note
                  - paragraph [ref=e557]: Option is experimental.
                - paragraph [ref=e558]:
                  - strong [ref=e559]: "--env"
                  - emphasis [ref=e560]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e561]:
                  - text: Active environment name (
                  - code [ref=e562]: ENV
                  - text: ). (default "default")
                - paragraph [ref=e563]:
                  - strong [ref=e564]: "--env-file"
                  - emphasis [ref=e565]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e566]:
                  - text: Path to environment settings file. Defaults to
                  - code [ref=e567]: $HOME/.config/temporalio/temporal.yaml
                  - text: .
                - paragraph [ref=e568]:
                  - strong [ref=e569]: "--grpc-meta"
                  - emphasis [ref=e570]: string[]
                - paragraph [ref=e571]:
                  - text: HTTP headers for requests. Format as a
                  - code [ref=e572]: KEY=VALUE
                  - text: pair. May be passed multiple times to set multiple headers. Can also be made available via environment variable as
                  - code [ref=e573]: TEMPORAL_GRPC_META_[name]
                  - text: .
                - paragraph [ref=e574]:
                  - strong [ref=e575]: "--identity"
                  - emphasis [ref=e576]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e577]:
                  - text: "The identity of the user or client submitting this request. Defaults to \"temporal-cli:"
                  - generic [ref=e578]:
                    - math [ref=e580]:
                      - generic [ref=e582]:
                        - generic [ref=e583]: U
                        - generic [ref=e584]: S
                        - generic [ref=e585]: E
                        - generic [ref=e586]: R
                        - generic [ref=e587]: "@"
                    - generic [ref=e589]: USER@
                  - text: HOST".
                - paragraph [ref=e590]:
                  - strong [ref=e591]: "--log-format"
                  - emphasis [ref=e592]: string-enum
                - paragraph [ref=e593]: "Log format. Accepted values: text, json. (default \"text\")"
                - paragraph [ref=e594]:
                  - strong [ref=e595]: "--log-level"
                  - emphasis [ref=e596]: string-enum
                - paragraph [ref=e597]:
                  - text: Log level. Default is "info" for most commands and "warn" for
                  - code [ref=e598]: server start-dev
                  - text: ". Accepted values: debug, info, warn, error, never. (default \"info\")"
                - paragraph [ref=e599]:
                  - strong [ref=e600]: "--namespace"
                  - text: ","
                  - strong [ref=e601]: "-n"
                  - emphasis [ref=e602]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e603]: Temporal Service Namespace. (default "default")
                - paragraph [ref=e604]:
                  - strong [ref=e605]: "--no-json-shorthand-payloads"
                  - emphasis [ref=e606]: bool
                - paragraph [ref=e607]: Raw payload output, even if the JSON option was used.
                - paragraph [ref=e608]:
                  - strong [ref=e609]: "--output"
                  - text: ","
                  - strong [ref=e610]: "-o"
                  - emphasis [ref=e611]: string-enum
                - paragraph [ref=e612]: "Non-logging data output format. Accepted values: text, json, jsonl, none. (default \"text\")"
                - paragraph [ref=e613]:
                  - strong [ref=e614]: "--profile"
                  - emphasis [ref=e615]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e616]: Profile to use for config file.
                - generic [ref=e617]:
                  - generic [ref=e618]:
                    - img [ref=e620]
                    - text: note
                  - paragraph [ref=e623]: Option is experimental.
                - paragraph [ref=e624]:
                  - strong [ref=e625]: "--time-format"
                  - emphasis [ref=e626]: string-enum
                - paragraph [ref=e627]: "Time format. Accepted values: relative, iso, raw. (default \"relative\")"
                - paragraph [ref=e628]:
                  - strong [ref=e629]: "--tls"
                  - emphasis [ref=e630]: bool
                - paragraph [ref=e631]: Enable base TLS encryption. Does not have additional options like mTLS or client certs. This is defaulted to true if api-key or any other TLS options are present. Use --tls=false to explicitly disable.
                - paragraph [ref=e632]:
                  - strong [ref=e633]: "--tls-ca-data"
                  - emphasis [ref=e634]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e635]: Data for server CA certificate. Can't be used with --tls-ca-path.
                - paragraph [ref=e636]:
                  - strong [ref=e637]: "--tls-ca-path"
                  - emphasis [ref=e638]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e639]: Path to server CA certificate. Can't be used with --tls-ca-data.
                - paragraph [ref=e640]:
                  - strong [ref=e641]: "--tls-cert-data"
                  - emphasis [ref=e642]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e643]: Data for x509 certificate. Can't be used with --tls-cert-path.
                - paragraph [ref=e644]:
                  - strong [ref=e645]: "--tls-cert-path"
                  - emphasis [ref=e646]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e647]: Path to x509 certificate. Can't be used with --tls-cert-data.
                - paragraph [ref=e648]:
                  - strong [ref=e649]: "--tls-disable-host-verification"
                  - emphasis [ref=e650]: bool
                - paragraph [ref=e651]: Disable TLS host-name verification.
                - paragraph [ref=e652]:
                  - strong [ref=e653]: "--tls-key-data"
                  - emphasis [ref=e654]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e655]: Private certificate key data. Can't be used with --tls-key-path.
                - paragraph [ref=e656]:
                  - strong [ref=e657]: "--tls-key-path"
                  - emphasis [ref=e658]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e659]: Path to x509 private key. Can't be used with --tls-key-data.
                - paragraph [ref=e660]:
                  - strong [ref=e661]: "--tls-server-name"
                  - emphasis [ref=e662]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e663]: Override target TLS server name.

                - paragraph [ref=e666]: "Delete a Workflow Executions and its Event History:"
                - generic [ref=e668]:
                  - code [ref=e670]:
                    - generic [ref=e671]: temporal workflow delete \
                    - generic [ref=e672]: "--workflow-id YourWorkflowId"

                    - generic [ref=e675]:
                      - img [ref=e676]
                      - img [ref=e678]
                - paragraph [ref=e680]: The removal executes asynchronously. If the Execution is Running, the Service terminates it before deletion.
                - paragraph [ref=e681]:
                  - text: Visit
                  - link "https://docs.temporal.io/visibility" [ref=e682] [cursor=pointer]:
                    - /url: https://docs.temporal.io/visibility
                  - text: to read more about Search Attributes and Query creation. See
                  - code [ref=e683]: temporal batch --help
                  - text: for a quick reference.
                - paragraph [ref=e684]: Use the following options to change the behavior of this command.
                - paragraph [ref=e685]:
                  - strong [ref=e686]: "Flags:"
                - paragraph [ref=e687]:
                  - strong [ref=e688]: "--query"
                  - text: ","
                  - strong [ref=e689]: "-q"
                  - emphasis [ref=e690]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e691]:
                  - text: Content for an SQL-like
                  - code [ref=e692]: QUERY
                  - text: List Filter. You must set either --workflow-id or --query.
                - paragraph [ref=e693]:
                  - strong [ref=e694]: "--reason"
                  - emphasis [ref=e695]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e696]: Reason for batch operation. Only use with --query. Defaults to user name.
                - paragraph [ref=e697]:
                  - strong [ref=e698]: "--rps"
                  - emphasis [ref=e699]: float
                - paragraph [ref=e700]: Limit batch's requests per second. Only allowed if query is present.
                - paragraph [ref=e701]:
                  - strong [ref=e702]: "--run-id"
                  - text: ","
                  - strong [ref=e703]: "-r"
                  - emphasis [ref=e704]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e705]: Run ID. Only use with --workflow-id. Cannot use with --query.
                - paragraph [ref=e706]:
                  - strong [ref=e707]: "--workflow-id"
                  - text: ","
                  - strong [ref=e708]: "-w"
                  - emphasis [ref=e709]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e710]: Workflow ID. You must set either --workflow-id or --query.

                  - emphasis [ref=e1015]: bool
                - paragraph [ref=e1016]: If set, disables loading environment config from config file.

                  - generic [ref=e1018]:
                    - img [ref=e1020]

                - paragraph [ref=e1024]:
                  - strong [ref=e1025]: "--env"
                  - emphasis [ref=e1026]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e1027]:
                  - text: Active environment name (
                  - code [ref=e1028]: ENV
                  - text: ). (default "default")
                - paragraph [ref=e1029]:

                  - emphasis [ref=e1031]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e1032]:
                  - text: Path to environment settings file. Defaults to
                  - code [ref=e1033]: $HOME/.config/temporalio/temporal.yaml
                  - text: .
                - paragraph [ref=e1034]:
                  - strong [ref=e1035]: "--grpc-meta"
                  - emphasis [ref=e1036]: string[]
                - paragraph [ref=e1037]:
                  - text: HTTP headers for requests. Format as a
                  - code [ref=e1038]: KEY=VALUE
                  - text: pair. May be passed multiple times to set multiple headers. Can also be made available via environment variable as
                  - code [ref=e1039]: TEMPORAL_GRPC_META_[name]
                  - text: .
                - paragraph [ref=e1040]:
                  - strong [ref=e1041]: "--identity"
                  - emphasis [ref=e1042]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e1043]:
                  - text: "The identity of the user or client submitting this request. Defaults to \"temporal-cli:"
                  - generic [ref=e1044]:
                    - math [ref=e1046]:
                      - generic [ref=e1048]:
                        - generic [ref=e1049]: U
                        - generic [ref=e1050]: S

                        - generic [ref=e1053]: "@"
                    - generic [ref=e1055]: USER@
                  - text: HOST".

                - paragraph [ref=e1060]:
                  - strong [ref=e1061]: "--log-level"
                  - emphasis [ref=e1062]: string-enum
                - paragraph [ref=e1063]:

                  - emphasis [ref=e1068]: string

                  - strong [ref=e1071]: "--no-json-shorthand-payloads"
                  - emphasis [ref=e1072]: bool
                - paragraph [ref=e1073]: Raw payload output, even if the JSON option was used.

                  - emphasis [ref=e1092]: string-enum
                - paragraph [ref=e1093]: "Time format. Accepted values: relative, iso, raw. (default \"relative\")"
                - paragraph [ref=e1094]:
                  - strong [ref=e1095]: "--tls"
                  - emphasis [ref=e1096]: bool
                - paragraph [ref=e1097]: Enable base TLS encryption. Does not have additional options like mTLS or client certs. This is defaulted to true if api-key or any other TLS options are present. Use --tls=false to explicitly disable.
                - paragraph [ref=e1098]:
                  - strong [ref=e1099]: "--tls-ca-data"
                  - emphasis [ref=e1100]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e1101]: Data for server CA certificate. Can't be used with --tls-ca-path.
                - paragraph [ref=e1102]:
                  - strong [ref=e1103]: "--tls-ca-path"
                  - emphasis [ref=e1104]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e1105]: Path to server CA certificate. Can't be used with --tls-ca-data.
                - paragraph [ref=e1106]:
                  - strong [ref=e1107]: "--tls-cert-data"
                  - emphasis [ref=e1108]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e1109]: Data for x509 certificate. Can't be used with --tls-cert-path.
                - paragraph [ref=e1110]:
                  - strong [ref=e1111]: "--tls-cert-path"
                  - emphasis [ref=e1112]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e1113]: Path to x509 certificate. Can't be used with --tls-cert-data.
                - paragraph [ref=e1114]:
                  - strong [ref=e1115]: "--tls-disable-host-verification"
                  - emphasis [ref=e1116]: bool
                - paragraph [ref=e1117]: Disable TLS host-name verification.
                - paragraph [ref=e1118]:
                  - strong [ref=e1119]: "--tls-key-data"
                  - emphasis [ref=e1120]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e1121]: Private certificate key data. Can't be used with --tls-key-path.
                - paragraph [ref=e1122]:
                  - strong [ref=e1123]: "--tls-key-path"
                  - emphasis [ref=e1124]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e1125]: Path to x509 private key. Can't be used with --tls-key-data.
                - paragraph [ref=e1126]:
                  - strong [ref=e1127]: "--tls-server-name"
                  - emphasis [ref=e1128]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e1129]: Override target TLS server name.

                - paragraph [ref=e1149]:
                  - text: Use
                  - code [ref=e1150]: "--event-details"
                  - text: to relay updates to the command-line output in JSON format. When using JSON output (
                  - code [ref=e1151]: "--output json"
                  - text: ), this includes the entire "history" JSON key for the run.
                - paragraph [ref=e1152]: Use the following options to change the behavior of this command.
                - paragraph [ref=e1153]:
                  - strong [ref=e1154]: "Flags:"
                - paragraph [ref=e1155]:
                  - strong [ref=e1156]: "--cron"
                  - emphasis [ref=e1157]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e1158]: Cron schedule for the Workflow.
                - paragraph [ref=e1159]:
                  - strong [ref=e1160]: "--detailed"
                  - emphasis [ref=e1161]: bool
                - paragraph [ref=e1162]: Display events as sections instead of table. Does not apply to JSON output.
                - paragraph [ref=e1163]:
                  - strong [ref=e1164]: "--execution-timeout"
                  - emphasis [ref=e1165]: duration
                - paragraph [ref=e1166]:
                  - text: Fail a WorkflowExecution if it lasts longer than
                  - code [ref=e1167]: DURATION
                  - text: . This time-out includes retries and ContinueAsNew tasks.
                - paragraph [ref=e1168]:
                  - strong [ref=e1169]: "--fail-existing"
                  - emphasis [ref=e1170]: bool
                - paragraph [ref=e1171]: Fail if the Workflow already exists.
                - paragraph [ref=e1172]:
                  - strong [ref=e1173]: "--fairness-key"
                  - emphasis [ref=e1174]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e1175]: Fairness key (max 64 bytes) for proportional task dispatch. Tasks with same key share capacity based on their weight.
                - paragraph [ref=e1176]:
                  - strong [ref=e1177]: "--fairness-weight"
                  - emphasis [ref=e1178]: float
                - paragraph [ref=e1179]: Weight [0.001-1000] for this fairness key. Keys are dispatched proportionally to their weights.
                - paragraph [ref=e1180]:
                  - strong [ref=e1181]: "--id-conflict-policy"
                  - emphasis [ref=e1182]: string-enum
                - paragraph [ref=e1183]: "Determines how to resolve a conflict when spawning a new Workflow Execution with a particular Workflow Id used by an existing Open Workflow Execution. Accepted values: Fail, UseExisting, TerminateExisting."
                - paragraph [ref=e1184]:
                  - strong [ref=e1185]: "--id-reuse-policy"
                  - emphasis [ref=e1186]: string-enum
                - paragraph [ref=e1187]: "Re-use policy for the Workflow ID in new Workflow Executions. Accepted values: AllowDuplicate, AllowDuplicateFailedOnly, RejectDuplicate, TerminateIfRunning."
                - paragraph [ref=e1188]:
                  - strong [ref=e1189]: "--input"
                  - text: ","
                  - strong [ref=e1190]: "-i"
                  - emphasis [ref=e1191]: string[]
                - paragraph [ref=e1192]: Input value. Use JSON content or set --input-meta to override. Can't be combined with --input-file. Can be passed multiple times to pass multiple arguments.
                - paragraph [ref=e1193]:
                  - strong [ref=e1194]: "--input-base64"
                  - emphasis [ref=e1195]: bool
                - paragraph [ref=e1196]: Assume inputs are base64-encoded and attempt to decode them.
                - paragraph [ref=e1197]:
                  - strong [ref=e1198]: "--input-file"
                  - emphasis [ref=e1199]: string[]
                - paragraph [ref=e1200]: A path or paths for input file(s). Use JSON content or set --input-meta to override. Can't be combined with --input. Can be passed multiple times to pass multiple arguments.
                - paragraph [ref=e1201]:
                  - strong [ref=e1202]: "--input-meta"
                  - emphasis [ref=e1203]: string[]
                - paragraph [ref=e1204]:
                  - text: Input payload metadata as a
                  - code [ref=e1205]: KEY=VALUE
                  - text: pair. When the KEY is "encoding", this overrides the default ("json/plain"). Can be passed multiple times. Repeated metadata keys are applied to the corresponding inputs in the provided order.
                - paragraph [ref=e1206]:
                  - strong [ref=e1207]: "--memo"
                  - emphasis [ref=e1208]: string[]
                - paragraph [ref=e1209]: Memo using 'KEY="VALUE"' pairs. Use JSON values.
                - paragraph [ref=e1210]:
                  - strong [ref=e1211]: "--priority-key"
                  - emphasis [ref=e1212]: int
                - paragraph [ref=e1213]: Priority key (1-5, lower numbers = higher priority). Tasks in a queue should be processed in close-to-priority-order. Default is 3 when not specified.
                - paragraph [ref=e1214]:
                  - strong [ref=e1215]: "--run-timeout"
                  - emphasis [ref=e1216]: duration
                - paragraph [ref=e1217]:
                  - text: Fail a Workflow Run if it lasts longer than
                  - code [ref=e1218]: DURATION
                  - text: .
                - paragraph [ref=e1219]:
                  - strong [ref=e1220]: "--search-attribute"
                  - emphasis [ref=e1221]: string[]
                - paragraph [ref=e1222]:
                  - text: Search Attribute in
                  - code [ref=e1223]: KEY=VALUE
                  - text: "format. Keys must be identifiers, and values must be JSON values. For example:"
                  - code [ref=e1224]: "'YourKey={\"your\": \"value\"}'"
                  - text: . Can be passed multiple times.
                - paragraph [ref=e1225]:
                  - strong [ref=e1226]: "--start-delay"
                  - emphasis [ref=e1227]: duration
                - paragraph [ref=e1228]: Delay before starting the Workflow Execution. Can't be used with cron schedules. If the Workflow receives a signal or update prior to this time, the Workflow Execution starts immediately.
                - paragraph [ref=e1229]:

                - paragraph [ref=e1453]: Send a message to a Workflow Execution to invoke an Update handler, and wait for the update to complete. If the Workflow Execution is not running, then a new workflow execution is started and the update is sent.
                - paragraph [ref=e1454]: Experimental.
                - generic [ref=e1456]:
                  - code [ref=e1458]:
                    - generic [ref=e1459]: temporal workflow execute-update-with-start \
                    - generic [ref=e1460]: "--update-name YourUpdate \\"
                    - generic [ref=e1461]: "--update-input '{\"update-key\": \"update-value\"}' \\"
                    - generic [ref=e1462]: "--workflow-id YourWorkflowId \\"
                    - generic [ref=e1463]: "--type YourWorkflowType \\"
                    - generic [ref=e1464]: "--task-queue YourTaskQueue \\"
                    - generic [ref=e1465]: "--id-conflict-policy Fail \\"
                    - generic [ref=e1466]: "--input '{\"wf-key\": \"wf-value\"}'"

                - paragraph [ref=e1477]:
                  - strong [ref=e1478]: "--cron"
                  - emphasis [ref=e1479]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e1480]: Cron schedule for the Workflow.
                - paragraph [ref=e1481]:
                  - strong [ref=e1482]: "--execution-timeout"
                  - emphasis [ref=e1483]: duration
                - paragraph [ref=e1484]:
                  - text: Fail a WorkflowExecution if it lasts longer than
                  - code [ref=e1485]: DURATION
                  - text: . This time-out includes retries and ContinueAsNew tasks.
                - paragraph [ref=e1486]:
                  - strong [ref=e1487]: "--fail-existing"
                  - emphasis [ref=e1488]: bool
                - paragraph [ref=e1489]: Fail if the Workflow already exists.
                - paragraph [ref=e1490]:
                  - strong [ref=e1491]: "--fairness-key"
                  - emphasis [ref=e1492]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e1493]: Fairness key (max 64 bytes) for proportional task dispatch. Tasks with same key share capacity based on their weight.
                - paragraph [ref=e1494]:
                  - strong [ref=e1495]: "--fairness-weight"
                  - emphasis [ref=e1496]: float
                - paragraph [ref=e1497]: Weight [0.001-1000] for this fairness key. Keys are dispatched proportionally to their weights.
                - paragraph [ref=e1498]:
                  - strong [ref=e1499]: "--id-conflict-policy"
                  - emphasis [ref=e1500]: string-enum
                - paragraph [ref=e1501]: "Determines how to resolve a conflict when spawning a new Workflow Execution with a particular Workflow Id used by an existing Open Workflow Execution. Accepted values: Fail, UseExisting, TerminateExisting."
                - paragraph [ref=e1502]:
                  - strong [ref=e1503]: "--id-reuse-policy"
                  - emphasis [ref=e1504]: string-enum
                - paragraph [ref=e1505]: "Re-use policy for the Workflow ID in new Workflow Executions. Accepted values: AllowDuplicate, AllowDuplicateFailedOnly, RejectDuplicate, TerminateIfRunning."
                - paragraph [ref=e1506]:
                  - strong [ref=e1507]: "--input"
                  - text: ","
                  - strong [ref=e1508]: "-i"
                  - emphasis [ref=e1509]: string[]
                - paragraph [ref=e1510]: Input value. Use JSON content or set --input-meta to override. Can't be combined with --input-file. Can be passed multiple times to pass multiple arguments.
                - paragraph [ref=e1511]:
                  - strong [ref=e1512]: "--input-base64"
                  - emphasis [ref=e1513]: bool
                - paragraph [ref=e1514]: Assume inputs are base64-encoded and attempt to decode them.
                - paragraph [ref=e1515]:
                  - strong [ref=e1516]: "--input-file"
                  - emphasis [ref=e1517]: string[]
                - paragraph [ref=e1518]: A path or paths for input file(s). Use JSON content or set --input-meta to override. Can't be combined with --input. Can be passed multiple times to pass multiple arguments.
                - paragraph [ref=e1519]:
                  - strong [ref=e1520]: "--input-meta"
                  - emphasis [ref=e1521]: string[]
                - paragraph [ref=e1522]:
                  - text: Input payload metadata as a
                  - code [ref=e1523]: KEY=VALUE
                  - text: pair. When the KEY is "encoding", this overrides the default ("json/plain"). Can be passed multiple times. Repeated metadata keys are applied to the corresponding inputs in the provided order.
                - paragraph [ref=e1524]:
                  - strong [ref=e1525]: "--memo"
                  - emphasis [ref=e1526]: string[]
                - paragraph [ref=e1527]: Memo using 'KEY="VALUE"' pairs. Use JSON values.
                - paragraph [ref=e1528]:
                  - strong [ref=e1529]: "--priority-key"
                  - emphasis [ref=e1530]: int
                - paragraph [ref=e1531]: Priority key (1-5, lower numbers = higher priority). Tasks in a queue should be processed in close-to-priority-order. Default is 3 when not specified.
                - paragraph [ref=e1532]:
                  - strong [ref=e1533]: "--run-id"
                  - text: ","
                  - strong [ref=e1534]: "-r"
                  - emphasis [ref=e1535]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e1536]: Run ID. If unset, looks for an Update against the currently-running Workflow Execution.
                - paragraph [ref=e1537]:
                  - strong [ref=e1538]: "--run-timeout"
                  - emphasis [ref=e1539]: duration
                - paragraph [ref=e1540]:
                  - text: Fail a Workflow Run if it lasts longer than
                  - code [ref=e1541]: DURATION
                  - text: .
                - paragraph [ref=e1542]:
                  - strong [ref=e1543]: "--search-attribute"
                  - emphasis [ref=e1544]: string[]
                - paragraph [ref=e1545]:
                  - text: Search Attribute in
                  - code [ref=e1546]: KEY=VALUE
                  - text: "format. Keys must be identifiers, and values must be JSON values. For example:"
                  - code [ref=e1547]: "'YourKey={\"your\": \"value\"}'"
                  - text: . Can be passed multiple times.
                - paragraph [ref=e1548]:
                  - strong [ref=e1549]: "--start-delay"
                  - emphasis [ref=e1550]: duration
                - paragraph [ref=e1551]: Delay before starting the Workflow Execution. Can't be used with cron schedules. If the Workflow receives a signal or update prior to this time, the Workflow Execution starts immediately.
                - paragraph [ref=e1552]:

                  - emphasis [ref=e1554]: string

                - paragraph [ref=e1953]: Temporal Service Namespace. (default "default")
                - paragraph [ref=e1954]:
                  - strong [ref=e1955]: "--no-json-shorthand-payloads"
                  - emphasis [ref=e1956]: bool
                - paragraph [ref=e1957]: Raw payload output, even if the JSON option was used.
                - paragraph [ref=e1958]:
                  - strong [ref=e1959]: "--output"
                  - text: ","
                  - strong [ref=e1960]: "-o"
                  - emphasis [ref=e1961]: string-enum
                - paragraph [ref=e1962]: "Non-logging data output format. Accepted values: text, json, jsonl, none. (default \"text\")"
                - paragraph [ref=e1963]:
                  - strong [ref=e1964]: "--profile"
                  - emphasis [ref=e1965]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e1966]: Profile to use for config file.
                - generic [ref=e1967]:
                  - generic [ref=e1968]:
                    - img [ref=e1970]
                    - text: note
                  - paragraph [ref=e1973]: Option is experimental.
                - paragraph [ref=e1974]:
                  - strong [ref=e1975]: "--time-format"
                  - emphasis [ref=e1976]: string-enum
                - paragraph [ref=e1977]: "Time format. Accepted values: relative, iso, raw. (default \"relative\")"
                - paragraph [ref=e1978]:
                  - strong [ref=e1979]: "--tls"
                  - emphasis [ref=e1980]: bool
                - paragraph [ref=e1981]: Enable base TLS encryption. Does not have additional options like mTLS or client certs. This is defaulted to true if api-key or any other TLS options are present. Use --tls=false to explicitly disable.
                - paragraph [ref=e1982]:
                  - strong [ref=e1983]: "--tls-ca-data"
                  - emphasis [ref=e1984]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e1985]: Data for server CA certificate. Can't be used with --tls-ca-path.
                - paragraph [ref=e1986]:
                  - strong [ref=e1987]: "--tls-ca-path"
                  - emphasis [ref=e1988]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e1989]: Path to server CA certificate. Can't be used with --tls-ca-data.
                - paragraph [ref=e1990]:
                  - strong [ref=e1991]: "--tls-cert-data"
                  - emphasis [ref=e1992]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e1993]: Data for x509 certificate. Can't be used with --tls-cert-path.
                - paragraph [ref=e1994]:
                  - strong [ref=e1995]: "--tls-cert-path"
                  - emphasis [ref=e1996]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e1997]: Path to x509 certificate. Can't be used with --tls-cert-data.
                - paragraph [ref=e1998]:
                  - strong [ref=e1999]: "--tls-disable-host-verification"
                  - emphasis [ref=e2000]: bool
                - paragraph [ref=e2001]: Disable TLS host-name verification.
                - paragraph [ref=e2002]:
                  - strong [ref=e2003]: "--tls-key-data"
                  - emphasis [ref=e2004]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e2005]: Private certificate key data. Can't be used with --tls-key-path.
                - paragraph [ref=e2006]:
                  - strong [ref=e2007]: "--tls-key-path"
                  - emphasis [ref=e2008]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e2009]: Path to x509 private key. Can't be used with --tls-key-data.
                - paragraph [ref=e2010]:
                  - strong [ref=e2011]: "--tls-server-name"
                  - emphasis [ref=e2012]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e2013]: Override target TLS server name.

                - paragraph [ref=e2455]:
                  - strong [ref=e2456]: "--tls-disable-host-verification"
                  - emphasis [ref=e2457]: bool
                - paragraph [ref=e2458]: Disable TLS host-name verification.
                - paragraph [ref=e2459]:
                  - strong [ref=e2460]: "--tls-key-data"
                  - emphasis [ref=e2461]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e2462]: Private certificate key data. Can't be used with --tls-key-path.
                - paragraph [ref=e2463]:
                  - strong [ref=e2464]: "--tls-key-path"
                  - emphasis [ref=e2465]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e2466]: Path to x509 private key. Can't be used with --tls-key-data.
                - paragraph [ref=e2467]:
                  - strong [ref=e2468]: "--tls-server-name"
                  - emphasis [ref=e2469]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e2470]: Override target TLS server name.

                - paragraph [ref=e2473]: "Send a Query to a Workflow Execution by Workflow ID to retrieve its state. This synchronous operation exposes the internal state of a running Workflow Execution, which constantly changes. You can query both running and completed Workflow Executions:"

                - paragraph [ref=e2489]: Use the following options to change the behavior of this command.
                - paragraph [ref=e2490]:
                  - strong [ref=e2491]: "Flags:"
                - paragraph [ref=e2492]:
                  - strong [ref=e2493]: "--input"
                  - text: ","
                  - strong [ref=e2494]: "-i"
                  - emphasis [ref=e2495]: string[]
                - paragraph [ref=e2496]: Input value. Use JSON content or set --input-meta to override. Can't be combined with --input-file. Can be passed multiple times to pass multiple arguments.
                - paragraph [ref=e2497]:
                  - strong [ref=e2498]: "--input-base64"
                  - emphasis [ref=e2499]: bool
                - paragraph [ref=e2500]: Assume inputs are base64-encoded and attempt to decode them.
                - paragraph [ref=e2501]:
                  - strong [ref=e2502]: "--input-file"
                  - emphasis [ref=e2503]: string[]
                - paragraph [ref=e2504]: A path or paths for input file(s). Use JSON content or set --input-meta to override. Can't be combined with --input. Can be passed multiple times to pass multiple arguments.
                - paragraph [ref=e2505]:
                  - strong [ref=e2506]: "--input-meta"
                  - emphasis [ref=e2507]: string[]
                - paragraph [ref=e2508]:
                  - text: Input payload metadata as a
                  - code [ref=e2509]: KEY=VALUE
                  - text: pair. When the KEY is "encoding", this overrides the default ("json/plain"). Can be passed multiple times. Repeated metadata keys are applied to the corresponding inputs in the provided order.
                - paragraph [ref=e2510]:
                  - strong [ref=e2511]: "--name"
                  - emphasis [ref=e2512]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e2513]: Query Type/Name. Required.
                - paragraph [ref=e2514]:
                  - strong [ref=e2515]: "--reject-condition"

                  - strong [ref=e2564]: "--command-timeout"

                - paragraph [ref=e2566]: The command execution timeout. 0s means no timeout.

                  - code [ref=e2572]: $CONFIG_PATH

                  - code [ref=e2573]: $HOME/.config

                - paragraph [ref=e2932]: Disable TLS host-name verification.
                - paragraph [ref=e2933]:
                  - strong [ref=e2934]: "--tls-key-data"
                  - emphasis [ref=e2935]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e2936]: Private certificate key data. Can't be used with --tls-key-path.
                - paragraph [ref=e2937]:
                  - strong [ref=e2938]: "--tls-key-path"
                  - emphasis [ref=e2939]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e2940]: Path to x509 private key. Can't be used with --tls-key-data.
                - paragraph [ref=e2941]:
                  - strong [ref=e2942]: "--tls-server-name"
                  - emphasis [ref=e2943]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e2944]: Override target TLS server name.

                  - code [ref=e3018]: $CONFIG_PATH
                  - text: is defined as
                  - code [ref=e3019]: $HOME/.config
                  - text: on Unix, "$HOME/Library/Application Support" on macOS, and %AppData% on Windows.

                - paragraph [ref=e3378]:
                  - text: Send an asynchronous notification (Signal) to a running Workflow Execution by its Workflow ID. The Signal is written to the History. When you include
                  - code [ref=e3379]: "--input"
                  - text: ", that data is available for the Workflow Execution to consume:"
                - generic [ref=e3381]:
                  - code [ref=e3383]:
                    - generic [ref=e3384]: temporal workflow signal \
                    - generic [ref=e3385]: "--workflow-id YourWorkflowId \\"
                    - generic [ref=e3386]: "--name YourSignal \\"
                    - generic [ref=e3387]: "--input '{\"YourInputKey\": \"YourInputValue\"}'"
                  - button "Copy code to clipboard" [ref=e3389] [cursor=pointer]:
                    - generic [ref=e3390]:
                      - img [ref=e3391]
                      - img [ref=e3393]
                - paragraph [ref=e3395]:
                  - text: Visit
                  - link "https://docs.temporal.io/visibility" [ref=e3396] [cursor=pointer]:
                    - /url: https://docs.temporal.io/visibility
                  - text: to read more about Search Attributes and Query creation. See
                  - code [ref=e3397]: temporal batch --help
                  - text: for a quick reference.
                - paragraph [ref=e3398]: Use the following options to change the behavior of this command.
                - paragraph [ref=e3399]:
                  - strong [ref=e3400]: "Flags:"
                - paragraph [ref=e3401]:
                  - strong [ref=e3402]: "--input"
                  - text: ","
                  - strong [ref=e3403]: "-i"
                  - emphasis [ref=e3404]: string[]
                - paragraph [ref=e3405]: Input value. Use JSON content or set --input-meta to override. Can't be combined with --input-file. Can be passed multiple times to pass multiple arguments.
                - paragraph [ref=e3406]:
                  - strong [ref=e3407]: "--input-base64"
                  - emphasis [ref=e3408]: bool
                - paragraph [ref=e3409]: Assume inputs are base64-encoded and attempt to decode them.
                - paragraph [ref=e3410]:
                  - strong [ref=e3411]: "--input-file"
                  - emphasis [ref=e3412]: string[]
                - paragraph [ref=e3413]: A path or paths for input file(s). Use JSON content or set --input-meta to override. Can't be combined with --input. Can be passed multiple times to pass multiple arguments.
                - paragraph [ref=e3414]:
                  - strong [ref=e3415]: "--input-meta"
                  - emphasis [ref=e3416]: string[]
                - paragraph [ref=e3417]:
                  - text: Input payload metadata as a
                  - code [ref=e3418]: KEY=VALUE
                  - text: pair. When the KEY is "encoding", this overrides the default ("json/plain"). Can be passed multiple times. Repeated metadata keys are applied to the corresponding inputs in the provided order.
                - paragraph [ref=e3419]:
                  - strong [ref=e3420]: "--name"
                  - emphasis [ref=e3421]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e3422]: Signal name. Required.
                - paragraph [ref=e3423]:
                  - strong [ref=e3424]: "--query"
                  - text: ","
                  - strong [ref=e3425]: "-q"
                  - emphasis [ref=e3426]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e3427]:
                  - text: Content for an SQL-like
                  - code [ref=e3428]: QUERY
                  - text: List Filter. You must set either --workflow-id or --query.
                - paragraph [ref=e3429]:
                  - strong [ref=e3430]: "--reason"
                  - emphasis [ref=e3431]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e3432]: Reason for batch operation. Only use with --query. Defaults to user name.
                - paragraph [ref=e3433]:
                  - strong [ref=e3434]: "--rps"
                  - emphasis [ref=e3435]: float
                - paragraph [ref=e3436]: Limit batch's requests per second. Only allowed if query is present.
                - paragraph [ref=e3437]:
                  - strong [ref=e3438]: "--run-id"
                  - text: ","
                  - strong [ref=e3439]: "-r"
                  - emphasis [ref=e3440]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e3441]: Run ID. Only use with --workflow-id. Cannot use with --query.
                - paragraph [ref=e3442]:
                  - strong [ref=e3443]: "--workflow-id"
                  - text: ","
                  - strong [ref=e3444]: "-w"
                  - emphasis [ref=e3445]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e3446]: Workflow ID. You must set either --workflow-id or --query.
                - paragraph [ref=e3447]:
                  - strong [ref=e3448]: "--yes"
                  - text: ","
                  - strong [ref=e3449]: "-y"
                  - emphasis [ref=e3450]: bool
                - paragraph [ref=e3451]: Don't prompt to confirm signaling. Only allowed when --query is present.
                - paragraph [ref=e3452]:
                  - strong [ref=e3453]: "Global Flags:"
                - paragraph [ref=e3454]:
                  - strong [ref=e3455]: "--address"
                  - emphasis [ref=e3456]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e3457]: Temporal Service gRPC endpoint. (default "localhost:7233")
                - paragraph [ref=e3458]:
                  - strong [ref=e3459]: "--api-key"
                  - emphasis [ref=e3460]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e3461]: API key for request.
                - paragraph [ref=e3462]:
                  - strong [ref=e3463]: "--client-authority"
                  - emphasis [ref=e3464]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e3465]: Temporal gRPC client :authority pseudoheader.
                - paragraph [ref=e3466]:
                  - strong [ref=e3467]: "--client-connect-timeout"
                  - emphasis [ref=e3468]: duration
                - paragraph [ref=e3469]: The client connection timeout. 0s means no timeout.
                - paragraph [ref=e3470]:
                  - strong [ref=e3471]: "--codec-auth"
                  - emphasis [ref=e3472]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e3473]: Authorization header for Codec Server requests.
                - paragraph [ref=e3474]:
                  - strong [ref=e3475]: "--codec-endpoint"
                  - emphasis [ref=e3476]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e3477]: Remote Codec Server endpoint.
                - paragraph [ref=e3478]:
                  - strong [ref=e3479]: "--codec-header"
                  - emphasis [ref=e3480]: string[]
                - paragraph [ref=e3481]:
                  - text: HTTP headers for requests to codec server. Format as a
                  - code [ref=e3482]: KEY=VALUE
                  - text: pair. May be passed multiple times to set multiple headers.
                - paragraph [ref=e3483]:
                  - strong [ref=e3484]: "--color"
                  - emphasis [ref=e3485]: string-enum
                - paragraph [ref=e3486]: "Output coloring. Accepted values: always, never, auto. (default \"auto\")"
                - paragraph [ref=e3487]:
                  - strong [ref=e3488]: "--command-timeout"
                  - emphasis [ref=e3489]: duration
                - paragraph [ref=e3490]: The command execution timeout. 0s means no timeout.
                - paragraph [ref=e3491]:
                  - strong [ref=e3492]: "--config-file"
                  - emphasis [ref=e3493]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e3494]:
                  - text: File path to read TOML config from, defaults to
                  - code [ref=e3495]: $CONFIG_PATH/temporal/temporal.toml
                  - text: where
                  - code [ref=e3496]: $CONFIG_PATH
                  - text: is defined as
                  - code [ref=e3497]: $HOME/.config
                  - text: on Unix, "$HOME/Library/Application Support" on macOS, and %AppData% on Windows.
                - generic [ref=e3498]:
                  - generic [ref=e3499]:
                    - img [ref=e3501]
                    - text: note
                  - paragraph [ref=e3504]: Option is experimental.
                - paragraph [ref=e3505]:

                  - emphasis [ref=e3507]: bool
                - paragraph [ref=e3508]: If set, disables loading environment config from environment variables.

                - paragraph [ref=e3519]: If set, disables loading environment config from config file.

                  - generic [ref=e3521]:

                  - emphasis [ref=e3529]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e3530]:
                  - text: Active environment name (
                  - code [ref=e3531]: ENV
                  - text: ). (default "default")
                - paragraph [ref=e3532]:
                  - strong [ref=e3533]: "--env-file"
                  - emphasis [ref=e3534]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e3535]:
                  - text: Path to environment settings file. Defaults to
                  - code [ref=e3536]: $HOME/.config/temporalio/temporal.yaml
                  - text: .
                - paragraph [ref=e3537]:
                  - strong [ref=e3538]: "--grpc-meta"
                  - emphasis [ref=e3539]: string[]
                - paragraph [ref=e3540]:
                  - text: HTTP headers for requests. Format as a
                  - code [ref=e3541]: KEY=VALUE
                  - text: pair. May be passed multiple times to set multiple headers. Can also be made available via environment variable as
                  - code [ref=e3542]: TEMPORAL_GRPC_META_[name]
                  - text: .
                - paragraph [ref=e3543]:
                  - strong [ref=e3544]: "--identity"
                  - emphasis [ref=e3545]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e3546]:
                  - text: "The identity of the user or client submitting this request. Defaults to \"temporal-cli:"
                  - generic [ref=e3547]:

                    - generic [ref=e3558]: USER@
                  - text: HOST".

                - paragraph [ref=e3582]:

                  - emphasis [ref=e3584]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e3585]: Profile to use for config file.

                - paragraph [ref=e3597]:
                  - strong [ref=e3598]: "--tls"
                  - emphasis [ref=e3599]: bool
                - paragraph [ref=e3600]: Enable base TLS encryption. Does not have additional options like mTLS or client certs. This is defaulted to true if api-key or any other TLS options are present. Use --tls=false to explicitly disable.
                - paragraph [ref=e3601]:
                  - strong [ref=e3602]: "--tls-ca-data"
                  - emphasis [ref=e3603]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e3604]: Data for server CA certificate. Can't be used with --tls-ca-path.
                - paragraph [ref=e3605]:
                  - strong [ref=e3606]: "--tls-ca-path"
                  - emphasis [ref=e3607]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e3608]: Path to server CA certificate. Can't be used with --tls-ca-data.
                - paragraph [ref=e3609]:
                  - strong [ref=e3610]: "--tls-cert-data"
                  - emphasis [ref=e3611]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e3612]: Data for x509 certificate. Can't be used with --tls-cert-path.
                - paragraph [ref=e3613]:
                  - strong [ref=e3614]: "--tls-cert-path"
                  - emphasis [ref=e3615]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e3616]: Path to x509 certificate. Can't be used with --tls-cert-data.
                - paragraph [ref=e3617]:
                  - strong [ref=e3618]: "--tls-disable-host-verification"
                  - emphasis [ref=e3619]: bool
                - paragraph [ref=e3620]: Disable TLS host-name verification.
                - paragraph [ref=e3621]:
                  - strong [ref=e3622]: "--tls-key-data"
                  - emphasis [ref=e3623]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e3624]: Private certificate key data. Can't be used with --tls-key-path.
                - paragraph [ref=e3625]:
                  - strong [ref=e3626]: "--tls-key-path"
                  - emphasis [ref=e3627]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e3628]: Path to x509 private key. Can't be used with --tls-key-data.
                - paragraph [ref=e3629]:
                  - strong [ref=e3630]: "--tls-server-name"
                  - emphasis [ref=e3631]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e3632]: Override target TLS server name.
                - heading "signal-with-startDirect link to signal-with-start" [level=2] [ref=e3633]:
                  - text: signal-with-start
                  - link "Direct link to signal-with-start" [ref=e3634] [cursor=pointer]:
                    - /url: "#signal-with-start"
                    - text: "#"
                - paragraph [ref=e3635]: Send an asynchronous notification (Signal) to a Workflow Execution. If the Workflow Execution is not running or is not found, it starts the workflow then sends the signal.
                - generic [ref=e3637]:
                  - code [ref=e3639]:
                    - generic [ref=e3640]: temporal workflow signal-with-start \
                    - generic [ref=e3641]: "--signal-name YourSignal \\"
                    - generic [ref=e3642]: "--signal-input '{\"some-key\": \"some-value\"}' \\"
                    - generic [ref=e3643]: "--workflow-id YourWorkflowId \\"
                    - generic [ref=e3644]: "--type YourWorkflowType \\"
                    - generic [ref=e3645]: "--task-queue YourTaskQueue \\"
                    - generic [ref=e3646]: "--input '{\"some-key\": \"some-value\"}'"
                  - button "Copy code to clipboard" [ref=e3648] [cursor=pointer]:
                    - generic [ref=e3649]:
                      - img [ref=e3650]
                      - img [ref=e3652]
                - paragraph [ref=e3654]: Use the following options to change the behavior of this command.
                - paragraph [ref=e3655]:
                  - strong [ref=e3656]: "Flags:"
                - paragraph [ref=e3657]:
                  - strong [ref=e3658]: "--cron"
                  - emphasis [ref=e3659]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e3660]: Cron schedule for the Workflow.
                - paragraph [ref=e3661]:
                  - strong [ref=e3662]: "--execution-timeout"
                  - emphasis [ref=e3663]: duration
                - paragraph [ref=e3664]:
                  - text: Fail a WorkflowExecution if it lasts longer than
                  - code [ref=e3665]: DURATION
                  - text: . This time-out includes retries and ContinueAsNew tasks.
                - paragraph [ref=e3666]:
                  - strong [ref=e3667]: "--fail-existing"
                  - emphasis [ref=e3668]: bool
                - paragraph [ref=e3669]: Fail if the Workflow already exists.
                - paragraph [ref=e3670]:
                  - strong [ref=e3671]: "--fairness-key"
                  - emphasis [ref=e3672]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e3673]: Fairness key (max 64 bytes) for proportional task dispatch. Tasks with same key share capacity based on their weight.
                - paragraph [ref=e3674]:
                  - strong [ref=e3675]: "--fairness-weight"
                  - emphasis [ref=e3676]: float
                - paragraph [ref=e3677]: Weight [0.001-1000] for this fairness key. Keys are dispatched proportionally to their weights.
                - paragraph [ref=e3678]:
                  - strong [ref=e3679]: "--id-conflict-policy"
                  - emphasis [ref=e3680]: string-enum
                - paragraph [ref=e3681]: "Determines how to resolve a conflict when spawning a new Workflow Execution with a particular Workflow Id used by an existing Open Workflow Execution. Accepted values: Fail, UseExisting, TerminateExisting."
                - paragraph [ref=e3682]:
                  - strong [ref=e3683]: "--id-reuse-policy"
                  - emphasis [ref=e3684]: string-enum
                - paragraph [ref=e3685]: "Re-use policy for the Workflow ID in new Workflow Executions. Accepted values: AllowDuplicate, AllowDuplicateFailedOnly, RejectDuplicate, TerminateIfRunning."
                - paragraph [ref=e3686]:
                  - strong [ref=e3687]: "--input"
                  - text: ","
                  - strong [ref=e3688]: "-i"
                  - emphasis [ref=e3689]: string[]
                - paragraph [ref=e3690]: Input value. Use JSON content or set --input-meta to override. Can't be combined with --input-file. Can be passed multiple times to pass multiple arguments.
                - paragraph [ref=e3691]:
                  - strong [ref=e3692]: "--input-base64"
                  - emphasis [ref=e3693]: bool
                - paragraph [ref=e3694]: Assume inputs are base64-encoded and attempt to decode them.
                - paragraph [ref=e3695]:
                  - strong [ref=e3696]: "--input-file"
                  - emphasis [ref=e3697]: string[]
                - paragraph [ref=e3698]: A path or paths for input file(s). Use JSON content or set --input-meta to override. Can't be combined with --input. Can be passed multiple times to pass multiple arguments.
                - paragraph [ref=e3699]:
                  - strong [ref=e3700]: "--input-meta"
                  - emphasis [ref=e3701]: string[]
                - paragraph [ref=e3702]:
                  - text: Input payload metadata as a
                  - code [ref=e3703]: KEY=VALUE
                  - text: pair. When the KEY is "encoding", this overrides the default ("json/plain"). Can be passed multiple times. Repeated metadata keys are applied to the corresponding inputs in the provided order.
                - paragraph [ref=e3704]:
                  - strong [ref=e3705]: "--memo"
                  - emphasis [ref=e3706]: string[]
                - paragraph [ref=e3707]: Memo using 'KEY="VALUE"' pairs. Use JSON values.
                - paragraph [ref=e3708]:
                  - strong [ref=e3709]: "--priority-key"
                  - emphasis [ref=e3710]: int
                - paragraph [ref=e3711]: Priority key (1-5, lower numbers = higher priority). Tasks in a queue should be processed in close-to-priority-order. Default is 3 when not specified.
                - paragraph [ref=e3712]:
                  - strong [ref=e3713]: "--run-timeout"
                  - emphasis [ref=e3714]: duration
                - paragraph [ref=e3715]:
                  - text: Fail a Workflow Run if it lasts longer than
                  - code [ref=e3716]: DURATION
                  - text: .
                - paragraph [ref=e3717]:
                  - strong [ref=e3718]: "--search-attribute"
                  - emphasis [ref=e3719]: string[]
                - paragraph [ref=e3720]:
                  - text: Search Attribute in
                  - code [ref=e3721]: KEY=VALUE
                  - text: "format. Keys must be identifiers, and values must be JSON values. For example:"
                  - code [ref=e3722]: "'YourKey={\"your\": \"value\"}'"
                  - text: . Can be passed multiple times.
                - paragraph [ref=e3723]:
                  - strong [ref=e3724]: "--signal-input"
                  - emphasis [ref=e3725]: string[]
                - paragraph [ref=e3726]: Signal input value. Use JSON content or set --signal-input-meta to override. Can't be combined with --signal-input-file. Can be passed multiple times to pass multiple arguments.
                - paragraph [ref=e3727]:
                  - strong [ref=e3728]: "--signal-input-base64"
                  - emphasis [ref=e3729]: bool
                - paragraph [ref=e3730]: Assume signal inputs are base64-encoded and attempt to decode them.
                - paragraph [ref=e3731]:
                  - strong [ref=e3732]: "--signal-input-file"
                  - emphasis [ref=e3733]: string[]
                - paragraph [ref=e3734]: A path or paths for input file(s). Use JSON content or set --signal-input-meta to override. Can't be combined with --signal-input. Can be passed multiple times to pass multiple arguments.
                - paragraph [ref=e3735]:
                  - strong [ref=e3736]: "--signal-input-meta"
                  - emphasis [ref=e3737]: string[]
                - paragraph [ref=e3738]:
                  - text: Input signal payload metadata as a
                  - code [ref=e3739]: KEY=VALUE
                  - text: pair. When the KEY is "encoding", this overrides the default ("json/plain"). Can be passed multiple times.
                - paragraph [ref=e3740]:

                  - emphasis [ref=e3742]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e3743]: Signal name. Required.

                  - emphasis [ref=e3746]: duration
                - paragraph [ref=e3747]: Delay before starting the Workflow Execution. Can't be used with cron schedules. If the Workflow receives a signal or update prior to this time, the Workflow Execution starts immediately.

                  - strong [ref=e4212]: "--execution-timeout"
                  - emphasis [ref=e4213]: duration
                - paragraph [ref=e4214]:
                  - text: Fail a WorkflowExecution if it lasts longer than
                  - code [ref=e4215]: DURATION
                  - text: . This time-out includes retries and ContinueAsNew tasks.
                - paragraph [ref=e4216]:
                  - strong [ref=e4217]: "--fail-existing"
                  - emphasis [ref=e4218]: bool
                - paragraph [ref=e4219]: Fail if the Workflow already exists.
                - paragraph [ref=e4220]:
                  - strong [ref=e4221]: "--fairness-key"
                  - emphasis [ref=e4222]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e4223]: Fairness key (max 64 bytes) for proportional task dispatch. Tasks with same key share capacity based on their weight.
                - paragraph [ref=e4224]:
                  - strong [ref=e4225]: "--fairness-weight"
                  - emphasis [ref=e4226]: float
                - paragraph [ref=e4227]: Weight [0.001-1000] for this fairness key. Keys are dispatched proportionally to their weights.
                - paragraph [ref=e4228]:
                  - strong [ref=e4229]: "--id-conflict-policy"
                  - emphasis [ref=e4230]: string-enum
                - paragraph [ref=e4231]: "Determines how to resolve a conflict when spawning a new Workflow Execution with a particular Workflow Id used by an existing Open Workflow Execution. Accepted values: Fail, UseExisting, TerminateExisting."
                - paragraph [ref=e4232]:
                  - strong [ref=e4233]: "--id-reuse-policy"
                  - emphasis [ref=e4234]: string-enum
                - paragraph [ref=e4235]: "Re-use policy for the Workflow ID in new Workflow Executions. Accepted values: AllowDuplicate, AllowDuplicateFailedOnly, RejectDuplicate, TerminateIfRunning."
                - paragraph [ref=e4236]:
                  - strong [ref=e4237]: "--input"
                  - text: ","
                  - strong [ref=e4238]: "-i"
                  - emphasis [ref=e4239]: string[]
                - paragraph [ref=e4240]: Input value. Use JSON content or set --input-meta to override. Can't be combined with --input-file. Can be passed multiple times to pass multiple arguments.
                - paragraph [ref=e4241]:
                  - strong [ref=e4242]: "--input-base64"
                  - emphasis [ref=e4243]: bool
                - paragraph [ref=e4244]: Assume inputs are base64-encoded and attempt to decode them.
                - paragraph [ref=e4245]:
                  - strong [ref=e4246]: "--input-file"
                  - emphasis [ref=e4247]: string[]
                - paragraph [ref=e4248]: A path or paths for input file(s). Use JSON content or set --input-meta to override. Can't be combined with --input. Can be passed multiple times to pass multiple arguments.
                - paragraph [ref=e4249]:
                  - strong [ref=e4250]: "--input-meta"
                  - emphasis [ref=e4251]: string[]
                - paragraph [ref=e4252]:
                  - text: Input payload metadata as a
                  - code [ref=e4253]: KEY=VALUE
                  - text: pair. When the KEY is "encoding", this overrides the default ("json/plain"). Can be passed multiple times. Repeated metadata keys are applied to the corresponding inputs in the provided order.
                - paragraph [ref=e4254]:
                  - strong [ref=e4255]: "--memo"
                  - emphasis [ref=e4256]: string[]
                - paragraph [ref=e4257]: Memo using 'KEY="VALUE"' pairs. Use JSON values.

                  - strong [ref=e4259]: "--priority-key"
                  - emphasis [ref=e4260]: int
                - paragraph [ref=e4261]: Priority key (1-5, lower numbers = higher priority). Tasks in a queue should be processed in close-to-priority-order. Default is 3 when not specified.
                - paragraph [ref=e4262]:

                  - emphasis [ref=e4264]: duration

                  - text: "format. Keys must be identifiers, and values must be JSON values. For example:"
                  - code [ref=e4272]: "'YourKey={\"your\": \"value\"}'"
                  - text: . Can be passed multiple times.

                  - strong [ref=e4274]: "--start-delay"
                  - emphasis [ref=e4275]: duration
                - paragraph [ref=e4276]: Delay before starting the Workflow Execution. Can't be used with cron schedules. If the Workflow receives a signal or update prior to this time, the Workflow Execution starts immediately.

                - paragraph [ref=e4356]: The command execution timeout. 0s means no timeout.
