                  - strong [ref=e4358]: "--config-file"
                  - emphasis [ref=e4359]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e4360]:
                  - text: File path to read TOML config from, defaults to
                  - code [ref=e4361]: $CONFIG_PATH/temporal/temporal.toml
                  - text: where
                  - code [ref=e4362]: $CONFIG_PATH
                  - text: is defined as
                  - code [ref=e4363]: $HOME/.config
                  - text: on Unix, "$HOME/Library/Application Support" on macOS, and %AppData% on Windows.
                - generic [ref=e4364]:
                  - generic [ref=e4365]:
                    - img [ref=e4367]
                    - text: note
                  - paragraph [ref=e4370]: Option is experimental.
                - paragraph [ref=e4371]:
                  - strong [ref=e4372]: "--disable-config-env"
                  - emphasis [ref=e4373]: bool
                - paragraph [ref=e4374]: If set, disables loading environment config from environment variables.
                - generic [ref=e4375]:
                  - generic [ref=e4376]:
                    - img [ref=e4378]
                    - text: note
                  - paragraph [ref=e4381]: Option is experimental.
                - paragraph [ref=e4382]:
                  - strong [ref=e4383]: "--disable-config-file"
                  - emphasis [ref=e4384]: bool
                - paragraph [ref=e4385]: If set, disables loading environment config from config file.
                - generic [ref=e4386]:
                  - generic [ref=e4387]:
                    - img [ref=e4389]
                    - text: note
                  - paragraph [ref=e4392]: Option is experimental.
                - paragraph [ref=e4393]:
                  - strong [ref=e4394]: "--env"
                  - emphasis [ref=e4395]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e4396]:
                  - text: Active environment name (
                  - code [ref=e4397]: ENV
                  - text: ). (default "default")
                - paragraph [ref=e4398]:
                  - strong [ref=e4399]: "--env-file"
                  - emphasis [ref=e4400]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e4401]:
                  - text: Path to environment settings file. Defaults to
                  - code [ref=e4402]: $HOME/.config/temporalio/temporal.yaml
                  - text: .
                - paragraph [ref=e4403]:
                  - strong [ref=e4404]: "--grpc-meta"
                  - emphasis [ref=e4405]: string[]
                - paragraph [ref=e4406]:
                  - text: HTTP headers for requests. Format as a
                  - code [ref=e4407]: KEY=VALUE
                  - text: pair. May be passed multiple times to set multiple headers. Can also be made available via environment variable as
                  - code [ref=e4408]: TEMPORAL_GRPC_META_[name]
                  - text: .
                - paragraph [ref=e4409]:
                  - strong [ref=e4410]: "--identity"
                  - emphasis [ref=e4411]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e4412]:
                  - text: "The identity of the user or client submitting this request. Defaults to \"temporal-cli:"
                  - generic [ref=e4413]:
                    - math [ref=e4415]:
                      - generic [ref=e4417]:
                        - generic [ref=e4418]: U
                        - generic [ref=e4419]: S
                        - generic [ref=e4420]: E
                        - generic [ref=e4421]: R
                        - generic [ref=e4422]: "@"
                    - generic [ref=e4424]: USER@
                  - text: HOST".
                - paragraph [ref=e4425]:
                  - strong [ref=e4426]: "--log-format"
                  - emphasis [ref=e4427]: string-enum
                - paragraph [ref=e4428]: "Log format. Accepted values: text, json. (default \"text\")"
                - paragraph [ref=e4429]:
                  - strong [ref=e4430]: "--log-level"
                  - emphasis [ref=e4431]: string-enum
                - paragraph [ref=e4432]:
                  - text: Log level. Default is "info" for most commands and "warn" for
                  - code [ref=e4433]: server start-dev
                  - text: ". Accepted values: debug, info, warn, error, never. (default \"info\")"
                - paragraph [ref=e4434]:
                  - strong [ref=e4435]: "--namespace"
                  - text: ","
                  - strong [ref=e4436]: "-n"
                  - emphasis [ref=e4437]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e4438]: Temporal Service Namespace. (default "default")
                - paragraph [ref=e4439]:
                  - strong [ref=e4440]: "--no-json-shorthand-payloads"
                  - emphasis [ref=e4441]: bool
                - paragraph [ref=e4442]: Raw payload output, even if the JSON option was used.
                - paragraph [ref=e4443]:
                  - strong [ref=e4444]: "--output"
                  - text: ","
                  - strong [ref=e4445]: "-o"
                  - emphasis [ref=e4446]: string-enum
                - paragraph [ref=e4447]: "Non-logging data output format. Accepted values: text, json, jsonl, none. (default \"text\")"
                - paragraph [ref=e4448]:
                  - strong [ref=e4449]: "--profile"
                  - emphasis [ref=e4450]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e4451]: Profile to use for config file.
                - generic [ref=e4452]:
                  - generic [ref=e4453]:
                    - img [ref=e4455]
                    - text: note
                  - paragraph [ref=e4458]: Option is experimental.
                - paragraph [ref=e4459]:
                  - strong [ref=e4460]: "--time-format"
                  - emphasis [ref=e4461]: string-enum
                - paragraph [ref=e4462]: "Time format. Accepted values: relative, iso, raw. (default \"relative\")"
                - paragraph [ref=e4463]:
                  - strong [ref=e4464]: "--tls"
                  - emphasis [ref=e4465]: bool
                - paragraph [ref=e4466]: Enable base TLS encryption. Does not have additional options like mTLS or client certs. This is defaulted to true if api-key or any other TLS options are present. Use --tls=false to explicitly disable.
                - paragraph [ref=e4467]:
                  - strong [ref=e4468]: "--tls-ca-data"
                  - emphasis [ref=e4469]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e4470]: Data for server CA certificate. Can't be used with --tls-ca-path.
                - paragraph [ref=e4471]:
                  - strong [ref=e4472]: "--tls-ca-path"
                  - emphasis [ref=e4473]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e4474]: Path to server CA certificate. Can't be used with --tls-ca-data.
                - paragraph [ref=e4475]:
                  - strong [ref=e4476]: "--tls-cert-data"
                  - emphasis [ref=e4477]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e4478]: Data for x509 certificate. Can't be used with --tls-cert-path.
                - paragraph [ref=e4479]:
                  - strong [ref=e4480]: "--tls-cert-path"
                  - emphasis [ref=e4481]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e4482]: Path to x509 certificate. Can't be used with --tls-cert-data.
                - paragraph [ref=e4483]:
                  - strong [ref=e4484]: "--tls-disable-host-verification"
                  - emphasis [ref=e4485]: bool
                - paragraph [ref=e4486]: Disable TLS host-name verification.
                - paragraph [ref=e4487]:
                  - strong [ref=e4488]: "--tls-key-data"
                  - emphasis [ref=e4489]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e4490]: Private certificate key data. Can't be used with --tls-key-path.
                - paragraph [ref=e4491]:
                  - strong [ref=e4492]: "--tls-key-path"
                  - emphasis [ref=e4493]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e4494]: Path to x509 private key. Can't be used with --tls-key-data.
                - paragraph [ref=e4495]:
                  - strong [ref=e4496]: "--tls-server-name"
                  - emphasis [ref=e4497]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e4498]: Override target TLS server name.
                - heading "start-update-with-startDirect link to start-update-with-start" [level=2] [ref=e4499]:
                  - text: start-update-with-start
                  - link "Direct link to start-update-with-start" [ref=e4500] [cursor=pointer]:
                    - /url: "#start-update-with-start"
                    - text: "#"
                - paragraph [ref=e4501]: Send a message to a Workflow Execution to invoke an Update handler, and wait for the update to be accepted or rejected. If the Workflow Execution is not running, then a new workflow execution is started and the update is sent.
                - paragraph [ref=e4502]: Experimental.
                - generic [ref=e4504]:
                  - code [ref=e4506]:
                    - generic [ref=e4507]: temporal workflow start-update-with-start \
                    - generic [ref=e4508]: "--update-name YourUpdate \\"
                    - generic [ref=e4509]: "--update-input '{\"update-key\": \"update-value\"}' \\"
                    - generic [ref=e4510]: "--update-wait-for-stage accepted \\"
                    - generic [ref=e4511]: "--workflow-id YourWorkflowId \\"
                    - generic [ref=e4512]: "--type YourWorkflowType \\"
                    - generic [ref=e4513]: "--task-queue YourTaskQueue \\"
                    - generic [ref=e4514]: "--id-conflict-policy Fail \\"
                    - generic [ref=e4515]: "--input '{\"wf-key\": \"wf-value\"}'"
                  - button "Copy code to clipboard" [ref=e4517] [cursor=pointer]:
                    - generic [ref=e4518]:
                      - img [ref=e4519]
                      - img [ref=e4521]
                - paragraph [ref=e4523]: Use the following options to change the behavior of this command.
                - paragraph [ref=e4524]:
                  - strong [ref=e4525]: "Flags:"
                - paragraph [ref=e4526]:
                  - strong [ref=e4527]: "--cron"
                  - emphasis [ref=e4528]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e4529]: Cron schedule for the Workflow.
                - paragraph [ref=e4530]:
                  - strong [ref=e4531]: "--execution-timeout"
                  - emphasis [ref=e4532]: duration
                - paragraph [ref=e4533]:
                  - text: Fail a WorkflowExecution if it lasts longer than
                  - code [ref=e4534]: DURATION
                  - text: . This time-out includes retries and ContinueAsNew tasks.
                - paragraph [ref=e4535]:
                  - strong [ref=e4536]: "--fail-existing"
                  - emphasis [ref=e4537]: bool
                - paragraph [ref=e4538]: Fail if the Workflow already exists.
                - paragraph [ref=e4539]:
                  - strong [ref=e4540]: "--fairness-key"
                  - emphasis [ref=e4541]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e4542]: Fairness key (max 64 bytes) for proportional task dispatch. Tasks with same key share capacity based on their weight.
                - paragraph [ref=e4543]:
                  - strong [ref=e4544]: "--fairness-weight"
                  - emphasis [ref=e4545]: float
                - paragraph [ref=e4546]: Weight [0.001-1000] for this fairness key. Keys are dispatched proportionally to their weights.
                - paragraph [ref=e4547]:
                  - strong [ref=e4548]: "--id-conflict-policy"
                  - emphasis [ref=e4549]: string-enum
                - paragraph [ref=e4550]: "Determines how to resolve a conflict when spawning a new Workflow Execution with a particular Workflow Id used by an existing Open Workflow Execution. Accepted values: Fail, UseExisting, TerminateExisting."
                - paragraph [ref=e4551]:
                  - strong [ref=e4552]: "--id-reuse-policy"
                  - emphasis [ref=e4553]: string-enum
                - paragraph [ref=e4554]: "Re-use policy for the Workflow ID in new Workflow Executions. Accepted values: AllowDuplicate, AllowDuplicateFailedOnly, RejectDuplicate, TerminateIfRunning."
                - paragraph [ref=e4555]:
                  - strong [ref=e4556]: "--input"
                  - text: ","
                  - strong [ref=e4557]: "-i"
                  - emphasis [ref=e4558]: string[]
                - paragraph [ref=e4559]: Input value. Use JSON content or set --input-meta to override. Can't be combined with --input-file. Can be passed multiple times to pass multiple arguments.
                - paragraph [ref=e4560]:
                  - strong [ref=e4561]: "--input-base64"
                  - emphasis [ref=e4562]: bool
                - paragraph [ref=e4563]: Assume inputs are base64-encoded and attempt to decode them.
                - paragraph [ref=e4564]:
                  - strong [ref=e4565]: "--input-file"
                  - emphasis [ref=e4566]: string[]
                - paragraph [ref=e4567]: A path or paths for input file(s). Use JSON content or set --input-meta to override. Can't be combined with --input. Can be passed multiple times to pass multiple arguments.
                - paragraph [ref=e4568]:
                  - strong [ref=e4569]: "--input-meta"
                  - emphasis [ref=e4570]: string[]
                - paragraph [ref=e4571]:
                  - text: Input payload metadata as a
                  - code [ref=e4572]: KEY=VALUE
                  - text: pair. When the KEY is "encoding", this overrides the default ("json/plain"). Can be passed multiple times. Repeated metadata keys are applied to the corresponding inputs in the provided order.
                - paragraph [ref=e4573]:
                  - strong [ref=e4574]: "--memo"
                  - emphasis [ref=e4575]: string[]
                - paragraph [ref=e4576]: Memo using 'KEY="VALUE"' pairs. Use JSON values.
                - paragraph [ref=e4577]:
                  - strong [ref=e4578]: "--priority-key"
                  - emphasis [ref=e4579]: int
                - paragraph [ref=e4580]: Priority key (1-5, lower numbers = higher priority). Tasks in a queue should be processed in close-to-priority-order. Default is 3 when not specified.
                - paragraph [ref=e4581]:
                  - strong [ref=e4582]: "--run-id"
                  - text: ","
                  - strong [ref=e4583]: "-r"
                  - emphasis [ref=e4584]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e4585]: Run ID. If unset, looks for an Update against the currently-running Workflow Execution.
                - paragraph [ref=e4586]:
                  - strong [ref=e4587]: "--run-timeout"
                  - emphasis [ref=e4588]: duration
                - paragraph [ref=e4589]:
                  - text: Fail a Workflow Run if it lasts longer than
                  - code [ref=e4590]: DURATION
                  - text: .
                - paragraph [ref=e4591]:
                  - strong [ref=e4592]: "--search-attribute"
                  - emphasis [ref=e4593]: string[]
                - paragraph [ref=e4594]:
                  - text: Search Attribute in
                  - code [ref=e4595]: KEY=VALUE
                  - text: "format. Keys must be identifiers, and values must be JSON values. For example:"
                  - code [ref=e4596]: "'YourKey={\"your\": \"value\"}'"
                  - text: . Can be passed multiple times.
                - paragraph [ref=e4597]:
                  - strong [ref=e4598]: "--start-delay"
                  - emphasis [ref=e4599]: duration
                - paragraph [ref=e4600]: Delay before starting the Workflow Execution. Can't be used with cron schedules. If the Workflow receives a signal or update prior to this time, the Workflow Execution starts immediately.
                - paragraph [ref=e4601]:
                  - strong [ref=e4602]: "--static-details"
                  - emphasis [ref=e4603]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e4604]: Static Workflow details for human consumption in UIs. Uses Temporal Markdown formatting, may be multiple lines.
                - generic [ref=e4605]:
                  - generic [ref=e4606]:
                    - img [ref=e4608]
                    - text: note
                  - paragraph [ref=e4611]: Option is experimental.

                - paragraph [ref=e4615]: Static Workflow summary for human consumption in UIs. Uses Temporal Markdown formatting, should be a single line.
                - generic [ref=e4616]:

                - paragraph [ref=e4627]: Workflow Task queue. Required.
                - paragraph [ref=e4628]:
                  - strong [ref=e4629]: "--task-timeout"
                  - emphasis [ref=e4630]: duration
                - paragraph [ref=e4631]:
                  - text: Fail a Workflow Task if it lasts longer than
                  - code [ref=e4632]: DURATION
                  - text: . This is the Start-to-close timeout for a Workflow Task. (default "10s")
                - paragraph [ref=e4633]:
                  - strong [ref=e4634]: "--type"
                  - emphasis [ref=e4635]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e4636]: Workflow Type name. Required.
                - paragraph [ref=e4637]:
                  - strong [ref=e4638]: "--update-first-execution-run-id"
                  - emphasis [ref=e4639]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e4640]: Parent Run ID. The update is sent to the last Workflow Execution in the chain started with this Run ID.
                - paragraph [ref=e4641]:
                  - strong [ref=e4642]: "--update-id"
                  - emphasis [ref=e4643]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e4644]: Update ID. If unset, defaults to a UUID.
                - paragraph [ref=e4645]:
                  - strong [ref=e4646]: "--update-input"
                  - emphasis [ref=e4647]: string[]

                - paragraph [ref=e4649]:
                  - strong [ref=e4650]: "--update-input-base64"
                  - emphasis [ref=e4651]: bool
                - paragraph [ref=e4652]: Assume update inputs are base64-encoded and attempt to decode them.

                - paragraph [ref=e4656]: A path or paths for input file(s). Use JSON content or set --update-input-meta to override. Can't be combined with --update-input. Can be passed multiple times to pass multiple arguments.
                - paragraph [ref=e4657]:

                - paragraph [ref=e4660]:

                  - text: pair. When the KEY is "encoding", this overrides the default ("json/plain"). Can be passed multiple times.

                  - emphasis [ref=e4664]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e4665]: Update name. Required.
                - paragraph [ref=e4666]:
                  - strong [ref=e4667]: "--update-wait-for-stage"
                  - emphasis [ref=e4668]: string-enum
                - paragraph [ref=e4669]:
                  - text: Update stage to wait for. The only option is
                  - code [ref=e4670]: accepted
                  - text: ", but this option is required. This is to allow a future version of the CLI to choose a default value. Required. Accepted values: accepted."
                - paragraph [ref=e4671]:

                  - strong [ref=e4822]: "--tls"
                  - emphasis [ref=e4823]: bool
                - paragraph [ref=e4824]: Enable base TLS encryption. Does not have additional options like mTLS or client certs. This is defaulted to true if api-key or any other TLS options are present. Use --tls=false to explicitly disable.
                - paragraph [ref=e4825]:
                  - strong [ref=e4826]: "--tls-ca-data"
                  - emphasis [ref=e4827]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e4828]: Data for server CA certificate. Can't be used with --tls-ca-path.
                - paragraph [ref=e4829]:
                  - strong [ref=e4830]: "--tls-ca-path"
                  - emphasis [ref=e4831]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e4832]: Path to server CA certificate. Can't be used with --tls-ca-data.
                - paragraph [ref=e4833]:
                  - strong [ref=e4834]: "--tls-cert-data"
                  - emphasis [ref=e4835]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e4836]: Data for x509 certificate. Can't be used with --tls-cert-path.
                - paragraph [ref=e4837]:
                  - strong [ref=e4838]: "--tls-cert-path"
                  - emphasis [ref=e4839]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e4840]: Path to x509 certificate. Can't be used with --tls-cert-data.
                - paragraph [ref=e4841]:
                  - strong [ref=e4842]: "--tls-disable-host-verification"
                  - emphasis [ref=e4843]: bool
                - paragraph [ref=e4844]: Disable TLS host-name verification.
                - paragraph [ref=e4845]:
                  - strong [ref=e4846]: "--tls-key-data"
                  - emphasis [ref=e4847]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e4848]: Private certificate key data. Can't be used with --tls-key-path.
                - paragraph [ref=e4849]:
                  - strong [ref=e4850]: "--tls-key-path"
                  - emphasis [ref=e4851]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e4852]: Path to x509 private key. Can't be used with --tls-key-data.
                - paragraph [ref=e4853]:
                  - strong [ref=e4854]: "--tls-server-name"
                  - emphasis [ref=e4855]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e4856]: Override target TLS server name.
                - heading "terminateDirect link to terminate" [level=2] [ref=e4857]:
                  - text: terminate
                  - link "Direct link to terminate" [ref=e4858] [cursor=pointer]:
                    - /url: "#terminate"
                    - text: "#"
                - paragraph [ref=e4859]: "Terminate a Workflow Execution:"
                - generic [ref=e4861]:
                  - code [ref=e4863]:
                    - generic [ref=e4864]: temporal workflow terminate \
                    - generic [ref=e4865]: "--reason YourReasonForTermination \\"
                    - generic [ref=e4866]: "--workflow-id YourWorkflowId"
                  - button "Copy code to clipboard" [ref=e4868] [cursor=pointer]:
                    - generic [ref=e4869]:
                      - img [ref=e4870]
                      - img [ref=e4872]
                - paragraph [ref=e4874]:
                  - text: The reason is optional and defaults to the current user's name. The reason is stored in the Event History as part of the
                  - code [ref=e4875]: WorkflowExecutionTerminated
                  - text: event. This becomes the closing Event in the Workflow Execution's history.
                - paragraph [ref=e4876]: "Executions may be terminated in bulk via a visibility Query list filter:"
                - generic [ref=e4878]:
                  - code [ref=e4880]:
                    - generic [ref=e4881]: temporal workflow terminate \
                    - generic [ref=e4882]: "--query YourQuery \\"
                    - generic [ref=e4883]: "--reason YourReasonForTermination"
                  - button "Copy code to clipboard" [ref=e4885] [cursor=pointer]:
                    - generic [ref=e4886]:
                      - img [ref=e4887]
                      - img [ref=e4889]
                - paragraph [ref=e4891]:
                  - text: Workflow code cannot see or respond to terminations. To perform clean-up work in your Workflow code, use
                  - code [ref=e4892]: temporal workflow cancel
                  - text: instead.
                - paragraph [ref=e4893]:
                  - text: Visit
                  - link "https://docs.temporal.io/visibility" [ref=e4894] [cursor=pointer]:
                    - /url: https://docs.temporal.io/visibility
                  - text: to read more about Search Attributes and Query creation. See
                  - code [ref=e4895]: temporal batch --help
                  - text: for a quick reference.
                - paragraph [ref=e4896]: Use the following options to change the behavior of this command.
                - paragraph [ref=e4897]:
                  - strong [ref=e4898]: "Flags:"
                - paragraph [ref=e4899]:
                  - strong [ref=e4900]: "--query"
                  - text: ","
                  - strong [ref=e4901]: "-q"
                  - emphasis [ref=e4902]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e4903]:
                  - text: Content for an SQL-like
                  - code [ref=e4904]: QUERY
                  - text: List Filter. You must set either --workflow-id or --query.
                - paragraph [ref=e4905]:
                  - strong [ref=e4906]: "--reason"
                  - emphasis [ref=e4907]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e4908]: Reason for termination. Defaults to message with the current user's name.
                - paragraph [ref=e4909]:
                  - strong [ref=e4910]: "--rps"
                  - emphasis [ref=e4911]: float
                - paragraph [ref=e4912]: Limit batch's requests per second. Only allowed if query is present.
                - paragraph [ref=e4913]:
                  - strong [ref=e4914]: "--run-id"
                  - text: ","
                  - strong [ref=e4915]: "-r"
                  - emphasis [ref=e4916]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e4917]: Run ID. Can only be set with --workflow-id. Do not use with --query.
                - paragraph [ref=e4918]:
                  - strong [ref=e4919]: "--workflow-id"
                  - text: ","
                  - strong [ref=e4920]: "-w"
                  - emphasis [ref=e4921]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e4922]: Workflow ID. You must set either --workflow-id or --query.
                - paragraph [ref=e4923]:
                  - strong [ref=e4924]: "--yes"
                  - text: ","
                  - strong [ref=e4925]: "-y"
                  - emphasis [ref=e4926]: bool
                - paragraph [ref=e4927]: Don't prompt to confirm termination. Can only be used with --query.
                - paragraph [ref=e4928]:
                  - strong [ref=e4929]: "Global Flags:"
                - paragraph [ref=e4930]:
                  - strong [ref=e4931]: "--address"
                  - emphasis [ref=e4932]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e4933]: Temporal Service gRPC endpoint. (default "localhost:7233")
                - paragraph [ref=e4934]:
                  - strong [ref=e4935]: "--api-key"
                  - emphasis [ref=e4936]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e4937]: API key for request.
                - paragraph [ref=e4938]:
                  - strong [ref=e4939]: "--client-authority"
                  - emphasis [ref=e4940]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e4941]: Temporal gRPC client :authority pseudoheader.
                - paragraph [ref=e4942]:
                  - strong [ref=e4943]: "--client-connect-timeout"
                  - emphasis [ref=e4944]: duration
                - paragraph [ref=e4945]: The client connection timeout. 0s means no timeout.
                - paragraph [ref=e4946]:
                  - strong [ref=e4947]: "--codec-auth"
                  - emphasis [ref=e4948]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e4949]: Authorization header for Codec Server requests.
                - paragraph [ref=e4950]:
                  - strong [ref=e4951]: "--codec-endpoint"
                  - emphasis [ref=e4952]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e4953]: Remote Codec Server endpoint.
                - paragraph [ref=e4954]:
                  - strong [ref=e4955]: "--codec-header"
                  - emphasis [ref=e4956]: string[]
                - paragraph [ref=e4957]:
                  - text: HTTP headers for requests to codec server. Format as a
                  - code [ref=e4958]: KEY=VALUE
                  - text: pair. May be passed multiple times to set multiple headers.
                - paragraph [ref=e4959]:
                  - strong [ref=e4960]: "--color"
                  - emphasis [ref=e4961]: string-enum
                - paragraph [ref=e4962]: "Output coloring. Accepted values: always, never, auto. (default \"auto\")"
                - paragraph [ref=e4963]:
                  - strong [ref=e4964]: "--command-timeout"
                  - emphasis [ref=e4965]: duration
                - paragraph [ref=e4966]: The command execution timeout. 0s means no timeout.
                - paragraph [ref=e4967]:
                  - strong [ref=e4968]: "--config-file"
                  - emphasis [ref=e4969]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e4970]:
                  - text: File path to read TOML config from, defaults to
                  - code [ref=e4971]: $CONFIG_PATH/temporal/temporal.toml
                  - text: where
                  - code [ref=e4972]: $CONFIG_PATH
                  - text: is defined as
                  - code [ref=e4973]: $HOME/.config
                  - text: on Unix, "$HOME/Library/Application Support" on macOS, and %AppData% on Windows.
                - generic [ref=e4974]:
                  - generic [ref=e4975]:
                    - img [ref=e4977]

                  - emphasis [ref=e4983]: bool
                - paragraph [ref=e4984]: If set, disables loading environment config from environment variables.

                - paragraph [ref=e5307]:
                  - strong [ref=e5308]: "--tls-ca-path"
                  - emphasis [ref=e5309]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e5310]: Path to server CA certificate. Can't be used with --tls-ca-data.
                - paragraph [ref=e5311]:
                  - strong [ref=e5312]: "--tls-cert-data"
                  - emphasis [ref=e5313]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e5314]: Data for x509 certificate. Can't be used with --tls-cert-path.
                - paragraph [ref=e5315]:
                  - strong [ref=e5316]: "--tls-cert-path"
                  - emphasis [ref=e5317]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e5318]: Path to x509 certificate. Can't be used with --tls-cert-data.
                - paragraph [ref=e5319]:
                  - strong [ref=e5320]: "--tls-disable-host-verification"
                  - emphasis [ref=e5321]: bool
                - paragraph [ref=e5322]: Disable TLS host-name verification.
                - paragraph [ref=e5323]:
                  - strong [ref=e5324]: "--tls-key-data"
                  - emphasis [ref=e5325]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e5326]: Private certificate key data. Can't be used with --tls-key-path.
                - paragraph [ref=e5327]:
                  - strong [ref=e5328]: "--tls-key-path"
                  - emphasis [ref=e5329]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e5330]: Path to x509 private key. Can't be used with --tls-key-data.
                - paragraph [ref=e5331]:
                  - strong [ref=e5332]: "--tls-server-name"
                  - emphasis [ref=e5333]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e5334]: Override target TLS server name.
                - heading "updateDirect link to update" [level=2] [ref=e5335]:
                  - text: update
                  - link "Direct link to update" [ref=e5336] [cursor=pointer]:
                    - /url: "#update"
                    - text: "#"
                - paragraph [ref=e5337]: An Update is a synchronous call to a Workflow Execution that can change its state, control its flow, and return a result.

                - paragraph [ref=e5340]: Given a Workflow Execution and an Update ID, return information about its current status, including a result if it has finished.

                - paragraph [ref=e5355]: Use the following options to change the behavior of this command.
                - paragraph [ref=e5356]:
                  - strong [ref=e5357]: "Flags:"
                - paragraph [ref=e5358]:
                  - strong [ref=e5359]: "--run-id"
                  - text: ","
                  - strong [ref=e5360]: "-r"
                  - emphasis [ref=e5361]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e5362]: Run ID. If unset, updates the currently-running Workflow Execution.
                - paragraph [ref=e5363]:
                  - strong [ref=e5364]: "--update-id"
                  - emphasis [ref=e5365]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e5366]: Update ID. Must be unique per Workflow Execution. Required.
                - paragraph [ref=e5367]:
                  - strong [ref=e5368]: "--workflow-id"
                  - text: ","
                  - strong [ref=e5369]: "-w"
                  - emphasis [ref=e5370]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e5371]: Workflow ID. Required.
                - paragraph [ref=e5372]:
                  - strong [ref=e5373]: "Global Flags:"
                - paragraph [ref=e5374]:
                  - strong [ref=e5375]: "--address"
                  - emphasis [ref=e5376]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e5377]: Temporal Service gRPC endpoint. (default "localhost:7233")
                - paragraph [ref=e5378]:
                  - strong [ref=e5379]: "--api-key"
                  - emphasis [ref=e5380]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e5381]: API key for request.
                - paragraph [ref=e5382]:
                  - strong [ref=e5383]: "--client-authority"
                  - emphasis [ref=e5384]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e5385]: Temporal gRPC client :authority pseudoheader.
                - paragraph [ref=e5386]:
                  - strong [ref=e5387]: "--client-connect-timeout"
                  - emphasis [ref=e5388]: duration
                - paragraph [ref=e5389]: The client connection timeout. 0s means no timeout.
                - paragraph [ref=e5390]:
                  - strong [ref=e5391]: "--codec-auth"
                  - emphasis [ref=e5392]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e5393]: Authorization header for Codec Server requests.
                - paragraph [ref=e5394]:
                  - strong [ref=e5395]: "--codec-endpoint"
                  - emphasis [ref=e5396]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e5397]: Remote Codec Server endpoint.
                - paragraph [ref=e5398]:
                  - strong [ref=e5399]: "--codec-header"
                  - emphasis [ref=e5400]: string[]
                - paragraph [ref=e5401]:
                  - text: HTTP headers for requests to codec server. Format as a
                  - code [ref=e5402]: KEY=VALUE
                  - text: pair. May be passed multiple times to set multiple headers.
                - paragraph [ref=e5403]:
                  - strong [ref=e5404]: "--color"
                  - emphasis [ref=e5405]: string-enum
                - paragraph [ref=e5406]: "Output coloring. Accepted values: always, never, auto. (default \"auto\")"
                - paragraph [ref=e5407]:
                  - strong [ref=e5408]: "--command-timeout"
                  - emphasis [ref=e5409]: duration
                - paragraph [ref=e5410]: The command execution timeout. 0s means no timeout.
                - paragraph [ref=e5411]:
                  - strong [ref=e5412]: "--config-file"
                  - emphasis [ref=e5413]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e5414]:
                  - text: File path to read TOML config from, defaults to
                  - code [ref=e5415]: $CONFIG_PATH/temporal/temporal.toml
                  - text: where
                  - code [ref=e5416]: $CONFIG_PATH
                  - text: is defined as
                  - code [ref=e5417]: $HOME/.config
                  - text: on Unix, "$HOME/Library/Application Support" on macOS, and %AppData% on Windows.
                - generic [ref=e5418]:

                    - text: "#"
                - paragraph [ref=e5555]: Send a message to a Workflow Execution to invoke an Update handler, and wait for the update to complete or fail. You can also use this to wait for an existing update to complete, by submitting an existing update ID.
                - generic [ref=e5557]:
                  - code [ref=e5559]:
                    - generic [ref=e5560]: temporal workflow update execute \
                    - generic [ref=e5561]: "--workflow-id YourWorkflowId \\"
                    - generic [ref=e5562]: "--name YourUpdate \\"
                    - generic [ref=e5563]: "--input '{\"some-key\": \"some-value\"}'"
                  - button "Copy code to clipboard" [ref=e5565] [cursor=pointer]:
                    - generic [ref=e5566]:
                      - img [ref=e5567]
                      - img [ref=e5569]
                - paragraph [ref=e5571]: Use the following options to change the behavior of this command.
                - paragraph [ref=e5572]:
                  - strong [ref=e5573]: "Flags:"
                - paragraph [ref=e5574]:
                  - strong [ref=e5575]: "--first-execution-run-id"
                  - emphasis [ref=e5576]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e5577]: Parent Run ID. The update is sent to the last Workflow Execution in the chain started with this Run ID.
                - paragraph [ref=e5578]:
                  - strong [ref=e5579]: "--input"
                  - text: ","
                  - strong [ref=e5580]: "-i"
                  - emphasis [ref=e5581]: string[]
                - paragraph [ref=e5582]: Input value. Use JSON content or set --input-meta to override. Can't be combined with --input-file. Can be passed multiple times to pass multiple arguments.
                - paragraph [ref=e5583]:
                  - strong [ref=e5584]: "--input-base64"
                  - emphasis [ref=e5585]: bool
                - paragraph [ref=e5586]: Assume inputs are base64-encoded and attempt to decode them.
                - paragraph [ref=e5587]:
                  - strong [ref=e5588]: "--input-file"
                  - emphasis [ref=e5589]: string[]
                - paragraph [ref=e5590]: A path or paths for input file(s). Use JSON content or set --input-meta to override. Can't be combined with --input. Can be passed multiple times to pass multiple arguments.
                - paragraph [ref=e5591]:
                  - strong [ref=e5592]: "--input-meta"
                  - emphasis [ref=e5593]: string[]
                - paragraph [ref=e5594]:
                  - text: Input payload metadata as a
                  - code [ref=e5595]: KEY=VALUE
                  - text: pair. When the KEY is "encoding", this overrides the default ("json/plain"). Can be passed multiple times. Repeated metadata keys are applied to the corresponding inputs in the provided order.
                - paragraph [ref=e5596]:
                  - strong [ref=e5597]: "--name"
                  - emphasis [ref=e5598]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e5599]: Handler method name. Required.
                - paragraph [ref=e5600]:
                  - strong [ref=e5601]: "--run-id"
                  - text: ","
                  - strong [ref=e5602]: "-r"
                  - emphasis [ref=e5603]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e5604]: Run ID. If unset, looks for an Update against the currently-running Workflow Execution.
                - paragraph [ref=e5605]:
                  - strong [ref=e5606]: "--update-id"
                  - emphasis [ref=e5607]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e5608]: Update ID. If unset, defaults to a UUID.

                  - strong [ref=e5610]: "--workflow-id"

                  - strong [ref=e5611]: "-w"
                  - emphasis [ref=e5612]: string

                - paragraph [ref=e5786]: Private certificate key data. Can't be used with --tls-key-path.

                  - strong [ref=e5788]: "--tls-key-path"
                  - emphasis [ref=e5789]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e5790]: Path to x509 private key. Can't be used with --tls-key-data.

                  - strong [ref=e5792]: "--tls-server-name"
                  - emphasis [ref=e5793]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e5794]: Override target TLS server name.

                - paragraph [ref=e5819]: Run ID. If unset, updates the currently-running Workflow Execution.

                  - text: pair. May be passed multiple times to set multiple headers.

                  - strong [ref=e5865]: "--command-timeout"
                  - emphasis [ref=e5866]: duration
                - paragraph [ref=e5867]: The command execution timeout. 0s means no timeout.

                  - code [ref=e5873]: $CONFIG_PATH
                  - text: is defined as
                  - code [ref=e5874]: $HOME/.config
                  - text: on Unix, "$HOME/Library/Application Support" on macOS, and %AppData% on Windows.

                - paragraph [ref=e6012]:
                  - text: Send a message to a Workflow Execution to invoke an Update handler, and wait for the update to be accepted or rejected. You can subsequently wait for the update to complete by using
                  - code [ref=e6013]: temporal workflow update execute
                  - text: .
                - generic [ref=e6015]:
                  - code [ref=e6017]:
                    - generic [ref=e6018]: temporal workflow update start \
                    - generic [ref=e6019]: "--workflow-id YourWorkflowId \\"
                    - generic [ref=e6020]: "--name YourUpdate \\"
                    - generic [ref=e6021]: "--input '{\"some-key\": \"some-value\"}'"
                    - generic [ref=e6022]: "--wait-for-stage accepted"

                - paragraph [ref=e6030]: Use the following options to change the behavior of this command.
                - paragraph [ref=e6031]:
                  - strong [ref=e6032]: "Flags:"
                - paragraph [ref=e6033]:
                  - strong [ref=e6034]: "--first-execution-run-id"
                  - emphasis [ref=e6035]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e6036]: Parent Run ID. The update is sent to the last Workflow Execution in the chain started with this Run ID.
                - paragraph [ref=e6037]:
                  - strong [ref=e6038]: "--input"
                  - text: ","
                  - strong [ref=e6039]: "-i"
                  - emphasis [ref=e6040]: string[]
                - paragraph [ref=e6041]: Input value. Use JSON content or set --input-meta to override. Can't be combined with --input-file. Can be passed multiple times to pass multiple arguments.
                - paragraph [ref=e6042]:
                  - strong [ref=e6043]: "--input-base64"
                  - emphasis [ref=e6044]: bool
                - paragraph [ref=e6045]: Assume inputs are base64-encoded and attempt to decode them.
                - paragraph [ref=e6046]:
                  - strong [ref=e6047]: "--input-file"
                  - emphasis [ref=e6048]: string[]
                - paragraph [ref=e6049]: A path or paths for input file(s). Use JSON content or set --input-meta to override. Can't be combined with --input. Can be passed multiple times to pass multiple arguments.
                - paragraph [ref=e6050]:
                  - strong [ref=e6051]: "--input-meta"
                  - emphasis [ref=e6052]: string[]
                - paragraph [ref=e6053]:
                  - text: Input payload metadata as a
                  - code [ref=e6054]: KEY=VALUE
                  - text: pair. When the KEY is "encoding", this overrides the default ("json/plain"). Can be passed multiple times. Repeated metadata keys are applied to the corresponding inputs in the provided order.
                - paragraph [ref=e6055]:
                  - strong [ref=e6056]: "--name"
                  - emphasis [ref=e6057]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e6058]: Handler method name. Required.
                - paragraph [ref=e6059]:
                  - strong [ref=e6060]: "--run-id"
                  - text: ","
                  - strong [ref=e6061]: "-r"
                  - emphasis [ref=e6062]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e6063]: Run ID. If unset, looks for an Update against the currently-running Workflow Execution.
                - paragraph [ref=e6064]:
                  - strong [ref=e6065]: "--update-id"
                  - emphasis [ref=e6066]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e6067]: Update ID. If unset, defaults to a UUID.
                - paragraph [ref=e6068]:
                  - strong [ref=e6069]: "--wait-for-stage"
                  - emphasis [ref=e6070]: string-enum
                - paragraph [ref=e6071]:
                  - text: Update stage to wait for. The only option is
                  - code [ref=e6072]: accepted
                  - text: ", but this option is required. This is to allow a future version of the CLI to choose a default value. Required. Accepted values: accepted."
                - paragraph [ref=e6073]:
                  - strong [ref=e6074]: "--workflow-id"
                  - text: ","

                  - code [ref=e6264]:
                    - generic [ref=e6265]: +---------------------------------------------------------------------+
                    - generic [ref=e6266]: "| CAUTION: Worflow update-options is experimental. Workflow Execution |"
                    - generic [ref=e6267]: "| properties are subject to change. |"
                    - generic [ref=e6268]: +---------------------------------------------------------------------+
                  - button "Copy code to clipboard" [ref=e6270] [cursor=pointer]:
                    - generic [ref=e6271]:
                      - img [ref=e6272]
                      - img [ref=e6274]
                - paragraph [ref=e6276]: "Modify properties of Workflow Executions:"
                - generic [ref=e6278]:
                  - code [ref=e6280]:
                    - generic [ref=e6281]: temporal workflow update-options [options]
                  - button "Copy code to clipboard" [ref=e6283] [cursor=pointer]:
                    - generic [ref=e6284]:
                      - img [ref=e6285]
                      - img [ref=e6287]
                - paragraph [ref=e6289]: It can override the Worker Deployment configuration of a Workflow Execution, which controls Worker Versioning.
                - paragraph [ref=e6290]:
                  - text: For example, to force Workers in the current Deployment execute the next Workflow Task change behavior to
                  - code [ref=e6291]: auto_upgrade
                  - text: ":"
                - generic [ref=e6293]:
                  - code [ref=e6295]:
                    - generic [ref=e6296]: temporal workflow update-options \
                    - generic [ref=e6297]: "--workflow-id YourWorkflowId \\"
                    - generic [ref=e6298]: "--versioning-override-behavior auto_upgrade"
                  - button "Copy code to clipboard" [ref=e6300] [cursor=pointer]:
                    - generic [ref=e6301]:
                      - img [ref=e6302]
                      - img [ref=e6304]
                - paragraph [ref=e6306]:
                  - text: or to pin the workflow execution to a Worker Deployment, set behavior to
                  - code [ref=e6307]: pinned
                  - text: ":"
                - generic [ref=e6309]:
                  - code [ref=e6311]:
                    - generic [ref=e6312]: temporal workflow update-options \
                    - generic [ref=e6313]: "--workflow-id YourWorkflowId \\"
                    - generic [ref=e6314]: "--versioning-override-behavior pinned \\"
                    - generic [ref=e6315]: "--versioning-override-deployment-name YourDeploymentName \\"
                    - generic [ref=e6316]: "--versioning-override-build-id YourDeploymentBuildId"
                  - button "Copy code to clipboard" [ref=e6318] [cursor=pointer]:
                    - generic [ref=e6319]:
                      - img [ref=e6320]
                      - img [ref=e6322]
                - paragraph [ref=e6324]:
                  - text: To remove any previous overrides, set the behavior to
                  - code [ref=e6325]: unspecified
                  - text: ":"
                - generic [ref=e6327]:
                  - code [ref=e6329]:
                    - generic [ref=e6330]: temporal workflow update-options \
                    - generic [ref=e6331]: "--workflow-id YourWorkflowId \\"
                    - generic [ref=e6332]: "--versioning-override-behavior unspecified"
                  - button "Copy code to clipboard" [ref=e6334] [cursor=pointer]:
                    - generic [ref=e6335]:
                      - img [ref=e6336]
                      - img [ref=e6338]
                - paragraph [ref=e6340]:
                  - text: To see the current override use
                  - code [ref=e6341]: temporal workflow describe
                - paragraph [ref=e6342]: Use the following options to change the behavior of this command.
                - paragraph [ref=e6343]:
                  - strong [ref=e6344]: "Flags:"
                - paragraph [ref=e6345]:
                  - strong [ref=e6346]: "--query"
                  - text: ","
                  - strong [ref=e6347]: "-q"
                  - emphasis [ref=e6348]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e6349]:
                  - text: Content for an SQL-like
                  - code [ref=e6350]: QUERY
                  - text: List Filter. You must set either --workflow-id or --query.
                - paragraph [ref=e6351]:
                  - strong [ref=e6352]: "--reason"
                  - emphasis [ref=e6353]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e6354]: Reason for batch operation. Only use with --query. Defaults to user name.
                - paragraph [ref=e6355]:
                  - strong [ref=e6356]: "--rps"
                  - emphasis [ref=e6357]: float
                - paragraph [ref=e6358]: Limit batch's requests per second. Only allowed if query is present.
                - paragraph [ref=e6359]:
                  - strong [ref=e6360]: "--run-id"
                  - text: ","
                  - strong [ref=e6361]: "-r"
                  - emphasis [ref=e6362]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e6363]: Run ID. Only use with --workflow-id. Cannot use with --query.
                - paragraph [ref=e6364]:
                  - strong [ref=e6365]: "--versioning-override-behavior"
                  - emphasis [ref=e6366]: string-enum
                - paragraph [ref=e6367]: "Override the versioning behavior of a Workflow. Required. Accepted values: unspecified, pinned, auto_upgrade."
                - paragraph [ref=e6368]:
                  - strong [ref=e6369]: "--versioning-override-build-id"
                  - emphasis [ref=e6370]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e6371]:
                  - text: When overriding to a
                  - code [ref=e6372]: pinned
                  - text: behavior, specifies the Build ID of the version to target.
                - paragraph [ref=e6373]:
                  - strong [ref=e6374]: "--versioning-override-deployment-name"
                  - emphasis [ref=e6375]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e6376]:
                  - text: When overriding to a
                  - code [ref=e6377]: pinned
                  - text: behavior, specifies the Deployment Name of the version to target.
                - paragraph [ref=e6378]:
                  - strong [ref=e6379]: "--workflow-id"
                  - text: ","
                  - strong [ref=e6380]: "-w"
                  - emphasis [ref=e6381]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e6382]: Workflow ID. You must set either --workflow-id or --query.
                - paragraph [ref=e6383]:
                  - strong [ref=e6384]: "--yes"
                  - text: ","
                  - strong [ref=e6385]: "-y"
                  - emphasis [ref=e6386]: bool
                - paragraph [ref=e6387]: Don't prompt to confirm signaling. Only allowed when --query is present.
                - paragraph [ref=e6388]:
                  - strong [ref=e6389]: "Global Flags:"
                - paragraph [ref=e6390]:
                  - strong [ref=e6391]: "--address"
                  - emphasis [ref=e6392]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e6393]: Temporal Service gRPC endpoint. (default "localhost:7233")
                - paragraph [ref=e6394]:
                  - strong [ref=e6395]: "--api-key"
                  - emphasis [ref=e6396]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e6397]: API key for request.
                - paragraph [ref=e6398]:
                  - strong [ref=e6399]: "--client-authority"
                  - emphasis [ref=e6400]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e6401]: Temporal gRPC client :authority pseudoheader.
                - paragraph [ref=e6402]:
                  - strong [ref=e6403]: "--client-connect-timeout"
                  - emphasis [ref=e6404]: duration
                - paragraph [ref=e6405]: The client connection timeout. 0s means no timeout.
                - paragraph [ref=e6406]:
                  - strong [ref=e6407]: "--codec-auth"
                  - emphasis [ref=e6408]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e6409]: Authorization header for Codec Server requests.
                - paragraph [ref=e6410]:
                  - strong [ref=e6411]: "--codec-endpoint"
                  - emphasis [ref=e6412]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e6413]: Remote Codec Server endpoint.
                - paragraph [ref=e6414]:
                  - strong [ref=e6415]: "--codec-header"
                  - emphasis [ref=e6416]: string[]
                - paragraph [ref=e6417]:
                  - text: HTTP headers for requests to codec server. Format as a
                  - code [ref=e6418]: KEY=VALUE
                  - text: pair. May be passed multiple times to set multiple headers.
                - paragraph [ref=e6419]:
                  - strong [ref=e6420]: "--color"
                  - emphasis [ref=e6421]: string-enum
                - paragraph [ref=e6422]: "Output coloring. Accepted values: always, never, auto. (default \"auto\")"
                - paragraph [ref=e6423]:
                  - strong [ref=e6424]: "--command-timeout"
                  - emphasis [ref=e6425]: duration
                - paragraph [ref=e6426]: The command execution timeout. 0s means no timeout.
                - paragraph [ref=e6427]:
                  - strong [ref=e6428]: "--config-file"
                  - emphasis [ref=e6429]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e6430]:
                  - text: File path to read TOML config from, defaults to
                  - code [ref=e6431]: $CONFIG_PATH/temporal/temporal.toml
                  - text: where
                  - code [ref=e6432]: $CONFIG_PATH
                  - text: is defined as
                  - code [ref=e6433]: $HOME/.config
                  - text: on Unix, "$HOME/Library/Application Support" on macOS, and %AppData% on Windows.
                - generic [ref=e6434]:
                  - generic [ref=e6435]:
                    - img [ref=e6437]
                    - text: note
                  - paragraph [ref=e6440]: Option is experimental.
                - paragraph [ref=e6441]:
                  - strong [ref=e6442]: "--disable-config-env"
                  - emphasis [ref=e6443]: bool
                - paragraph [ref=e6444]: If set, disables loading environment config from environment variables.
                - generic [ref=e6445]:
                  - generic [ref=e6446]:
                    - img [ref=e6448]
                    - text: note
                  - paragraph [ref=e6451]: Option is experimental.
                - paragraph [ref=e6452]:
                  - strong [ref=e6453]: "--disable-config-file"
                  - emphasis [ref=e6454]: bool
                - paragraph [ref=e6455]: If set, disables loading environment config from config file.
                - generic [ref=e6456]:
                  - generic [ref=e6457]:
                    - img [ref=e6459]
                    - text: note
                  - paragraph [ref=e6462]: Option is experimental.
                - paragraph [ref=e6463]:
                  - strong [ref=e6464]: "--env"
                  - emphasis [ref=e6465]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e6466]:
                  - text: Active environment name (
                  - code [ref=e6467]: ENV
                  - text: ). (default "default")
                - paragraph [ref=e6468]:
                  - strong [ref=e6469]: "--env-file"
                  - emphasis [ref=e6470]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e6471]:
                  - text: Path to environment settings file. Defaults to
                  - code [ref=e6472]: $HOME/.config/temporalio/temporal.yaml
                  - text: .
                - paragraph [ref=e6473]:
                  - strong [ref=e6474]: "--grpc-meta"
                  - emphasis [ref=e6475]: string[]
                - paragraph [ref=e6476]:
                  - text: HTTP headers for requests. Format as a
                  - code [ref=e6477]: KEY=VALUE
                  - text: pair. May be passed multiple times to set multiple headers. Can also be made available via environment variable as
                  - code [ref=e6478]: TEMPORAL_GRPC_META_[name]
                  - text: .
                - paragraph [ref=e6479]:
                  - strong [ref=e6480]: "--identity"
                  - emphasis [ref=e6481]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e6482]:
                  - text: "The identity of the user or client submitting this request. Defaults to \"temporal-cli:"
                  - generic [ref=e6483]:
                    - math [ref=e6485]:
                      - generic [ref=e6487]:
                        - generic [ref=e6488]: U
                        - generic [ref=e6489]: S
                        - generic [ref=e6490]: E
                        - generic [ref=e6491]: R
                        - generic [ref=e6492]: "@"
                    - generic [ref=e6494]: USER@
                  - text: HOST".
                - paragraph [ref=e6495]:
                  - strong [ref=e6496]: "--log-format"
                  - emphasis [ref=e6497]: string-enum
                - paragraph [ref=e6498]: "Log format. Accepted values: text, json. (default \"text\")"
                - paragraph [ref=e6499]:
                  - strong [ref=e6500]: "--log-level"
                  - emphasis [ref=e6501]: string-enum
                - paragraph [ref=e6502]:
                  - text: Log level. Default is "info" for most commands and "warn" for
                  - code [ref=e6503]: server start-dev
                  - text: ". Accepted values: debug, info, warn, error, never. (default \"info\")"
                - paragraph [ref=e6504]:
                  - strong [ref=e6505]: "--namespace"
                  - text: ","
                  - strong [ref=e6506]: "-n"
                  - emphasis [ref=e6507]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e6508]: Temporal Service Namespace. (default "default")
                - paragraph [ref=e6509]:
                  - strong [ref=e6510]: "--no-json-shorthand-payloads"
                  - emphasis [ref=e6511]: bool
                - paragraph [ref=e6512]: Raw payload output, even if the JSON option was used.
                - paragraph [ref=e6513]:
                  - strong [ref=e6514]: "--output"
                  - text: ","
                  - strong [ref=e6515]: "-o"
                  - emphasis [ref=e6516]: string-enum
                - paragraph [ref=e6517]: "Non-logging data output format. Accepted values: text, json, jsonl, none. (default \"text\")"
                - paragraph [ref=e6518]:
                  - strong [ref=e6519]: "--profile"
                  - emphasis [ref=e6520]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e6521]: Profile to use for config file.
                - generic [ref=e6522]:
                  - generic [ref=e6523]:
                    - img [ref=e6525]
                    - text: note
                  - paragraph [ref=e6528]: Option is experimental.
                - paragraph [ref=e6529]:
                  - strong [ref=e6530]: "--time-format"
                  - emphasis [ref=e6531]: string-enum
                - paragraph [ref=e6532]: "Time format. Accepted values: relative, iso, raw. (default \"relative\")"
                - paragraph [ref=e6533]:
                  - strong [ref=e6534]: "--tls"
                  - emphasis [ref=e6535]: bool
                - paragraph [ref=e6536]: Enable base TLS encryption. Does not have additional options like mTLS or client certs. This is defaulted to true if api-key or any other TLS options are present. Use --tls=false to explicitly disable.
                - paragraph [ref=e6537]:
                  - strong [ref=e6538]: "--tls-ca-data"
                  - emphasis [ref=e6539]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e6540]: Data for server CA certificate. Can't be used with --tls-ca-path.
                - paragraph [ref=e6541]:
                  - strong [ref=e6542]: "--tls-ca-path"
                  - emphasis [ref=e6543]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e6544]: Path to server CA certificate. Can't be used with --tls-ca-data.
                - paragraph [ref=e6545]:
                  - strong [ref=e6546]: "--tls-cert-data"
                  - emphasis [ref=e6547]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e6548]: Data for x509 certificate. Can't be used with --tls-cert-path.
                - paragraph [ref=e6549]:
                  - strong [ref=e6550]: "--tls-cert-path"
                  - emphasis [ref=e6551]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e6552]: Path to x509 certificate. Can't be used with --tls-cert-data.
                - paragraph [ref=e6553]:
                  - strong [ref=e6554]: "--tls-disable-host-verification"
                  - emphasis [ref=e6555]: bool
                - paragraph [ref=e6556]: Disable TLS host-name verification.
                - paragraph [ref=e6557]:
                  - strong [ref=e6558]: "--tls-key-data"
                  - emphasis [ref=e6559]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e6560]: Private certificate key data. Can't be used with --tls-key-path.
                - paragraph [ref=e6561]:
                  - strong [ref=e6562]: "--tls-key-path"
                  - emphasis [ref=e6563]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e6564]: Path to x509 private key. Can't be used with --tls-key-data.
                - paragraph [ref=e6565]:
                  - strong [ref=e6566]: "--tls-server-name"
                  - emphasis [ref=e6567]: string
                - paragraph [ref=e6568]: Override target TLS server name.
              - generic [ref=e6569]:
                - generic [ref=e6571]:
